That woman must be one who can dedicate her life and everything else for God, not one who betrays God. She must be prepared to be punished and to perish.

Rebecca knew that Isaac was trying to bless her elder son Esau, so she told Jacob, "Your father is trying to bless your brother Esau," and had Jacob receive the blessing in place of Esau. This is a family struggle.

Isaac intended to bless Esau, and Esau went hunting to fulfill Isaac's wish. However, Jacob and Rebecca thought about the will of heaven in their inner selves. It was not for their own position. Rebecca was in a position to sacrifice herself for the will of heaven. Isaac sent Esau out hunting to bless him for his own good, but Rebecca was prepared to have Jacob receive the blessing even if it meant being chased away. Their emotional foundations were different.

Who caused this? It was not because of Isaac. It was also not because of Esau. It was to deny the men of the satanic world. It was to deny all the firstborn sons related to the satanic world. It means denying the firstborn husband and son. Do you understand what I mean?

Why did they do that? It was for the sake of the will. However, sending Esau out to hunt for the blessing was not denial. He sent Esau out from a position of self-affirmation. Therefore, in terms of emotional attitude, Rebecca was prepared for her own sacrifice. Even if I am chased away from this house, if my beloved son can inherit the lineage of heavenly blessing, I will do anything.

This is in line with the heart of the restoration providence.
God's restoration providence seeks to inherit His will on this earth, even if it means going through hardships and sacrifices. Therefore, by serving in a position aligned with the providential heart, it was possible to inherit God's will. Moreover, from a providential perspective, since the archangel led Eve to fall, Rebecca, who is in the position of Eve, indirectly deceived Isaac, who is in the position of the archangel, to achieve indemnification and restoration. By aligning all internal and external aspects, Jacob was able to receive God's blessing.

Rebecca fought in such a way that she ultimately loved Jacob, who was in the Abel position, more than her husband and her firstborn son Esau. This means that she took Jacob as a being of hope that she could not replace even if she gave up her husband or her firstborn son. This shows that a woman must have the emotional attitude to abandon her husband and children for the sake of the will to fulfill the purpose.

In this position, Rebecca established the foundation of the will by becoming one with Jacob. This signifies the future coming of Jesus and Mary. Mary, too, must not consider her parents, siblings, or environment if she is to fulfill the will. She must only keep the will in mind.

Women who have been examples in the history of restoration providence.
In Matthew chapter 1, there are four women mentioned. Among them, Bathsheba is the mother of Solomon. Did Bathsheba hate King David until the end? If she did, she could not be the mother of Solomon. King David sent her husband Uriah to war and planned to take her, but she accepted that as fate and, at the same time, believed that there was a great will in it. She thought that King David was not doing this for bad reasons but because there was some great purpose behind it. Moreover, she was a virtuous woman who prayed for the country to do well, even if it meant sacrificing her husband.

If Bathsheba had stood in a position of hating King David, she could never have given birth to a king like Solomon. If she had harbored a desire for revenge against King David, who killed her husband, Solomon could never have been born.
However, Bathsheba thought that even though her husband was dead, for him to be a loyal subject, he must willingly sacrifice not only himself but also his wife for the king. Therefore, Bathsheba treated King David with the belief that "Isn't it the duty of my husband to dedicate himself entirely to the king, with all his sincerity and integrity?" This is why King Solomon could be born here. Do you understand what I mean?

Next, when we look at the harlot Rahab, she was a woman of the street, yet how did she ascend to the genealogy of Jesus? It was because she hid the Israelite spies who had come to scout Jericho. At that time, Rahab was a tavern woman, but she risked her life to protect them. She prioritized protecting them over the men of her own nation. This represents the attitude that women should adopt in the future world of restoration.

Because she was in such a position, Rahab could inherit the heavenly lineage. It must have been because she was a woman of purpose, but she had a strong desire in her heart to "help these men at the risk of my life more than any other men." She held a deep commitment in her heart to become a necessary woman in front of a single hope, transcending her own position and circumstances. Despite being a foreign woman and knowing that the Israelite nation was her enemy, she recognized that they were a blessed nation and had the heart to cooperate and empathize with them. This thought must have always accompanied her throughout her life.

When we look at Ruth, she was living with her mother-in-law after her husband died, and her mother-in-law introduced her to Boaz as a concubine. In this situation, Ruth thought, "My mother-in-law is more concerned about my path than I am, and she cares for me more than I do for myself," and she followed her mother-in-law's advice. She considered everything about herself and chose the path of sacrifice. This is different from taking risks. This type of compliance will represent a typical woman in establishing purpose in the future. We need to understand this.

When we look at these issues, there is always a burden of mission on the path of faith. From now on, I believe there will be nothing adventurous in the path that the Unification Church itself must take. However, the journey we have walked until now has gone through processes that you cannot imagine.

The Importance of Leaders on the Path of Mission
Following the path of mission always involves internal struggles. It is the responsibility of the leader to navigate these internal struggles well. If a leader makes a mistake, it leads to failure. If a leader goes wrong, significant problems arise. Therefore, do not act rashly. Even when you see something good, do not be excessively joyful, and when you see something bad, do not be excessively sorrowful. At all times, you must correct your heart's attitude and cautiously discern right from wrong.

And because we do not know what might happen, you must never stand at the forefront. Even when carrying out tasks, you must proceed with a first operation, second operation, and third operation.

Restoration history is like that. Restoration history goes in reverse. It works through rebirth, growth, and completion. When viewed in relation to God, restoration history is about restoring Adam's sons and restoring Adam and God. In this way, restoration must occur through the three stages. Therefore, the God of Abraham, the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob emerged, and these three stages correspond to a single case. If this does not align, the purpose cannot be fulfilled.

So, what kind of strategy should be employed to fulfill the purpose? When focusing on the Teacher, the Teacher is in the position of completion, while you are in the position of sons, that is, in the position of growth. And those who are coming in now will be in the position of rebirth. Thus, there are three stages. Therefore, the Teacher will not stand at the forefront if possible. Just as there were the archangel and Adam before God, and just as there was the angelic world and humanity, the strategy must always be executed from this perspective.

When operating from this standpoint, the Teacher does not directly step forward. God works through the members. The important issue is to forewarn through the members and to implement the work; the commands are not given by me but are directed through the members.

If something goes wrong in this process, who is responsible? The Teacher does not take responsibility. Instead, the Teacher has the responsibility to guide the members when they go wrong. When a task fails and is reported to the Teacher, I can lead them. Therefore, correction is possible.

Until now, our church has operated in this way. The Teacher has not stood at the forefront. This is unavoidable for the overall safety operation. However, the leaders of general spiritual groups stand at the forefront and make a fuss. When a leader stands at the forefront, everything collides head-on. This is dangerous.

Now is the time to conduct internal maintenance.
In the pioneering era of the 1960s, the Teacher had no choice but to stand at the forefront. Thus, the Teacher faced things head-on. While it was dangerous for the Teacher to confront things directly, now that we are advancing indirectly, it is not dangerous. Here, we must have an ideology that can encompass everything.

To do this, we must receive reports from the members about what they have done and be able to assess them. It is essential to be able to discern whether the work was right or wrong. If you cannot assess whether the work was correct or not, you cannot manage that work. If you cannot manage that work, you cannot establish a relationship with me. After assigning tasks, you must receive reports about those tasks and continually assess whether the results were good or bad, gradually rising higher. This principle of development applies to you as well.

In the world of faith, comrades are necessary. Therefore, our Unification Church has an organization called the Three-Stage Team. This Three-Stage Team is an organization that helps each other in a messianic role. However, when you quietly observe, you find that you do not understand this value while living your faith. You live without knowing whether the Three-Stage Team has value or not.

The Three-Stage Team should become partners, confessing their faith lives and building a horizontal foundation together. If each person combines their unique experiences of grace to lay a foundation, development would occur quickly, yet you are unable to do this.

Therefore, you must take an interest in such issues moving forward. Moreover, starting this year, unlike in the past, the time has come for internal maintenance. Hence, I have sent the wives of blessed families to evangelize. If the wives have been sent out, what should the husbands do?

From a principled perspective, sending out all the wives of blessed families signifies that the time has come for women to take the lead. In the past, in the 1960s, when women took the lead, it was from an individual standpoint. This was because Eve took the lead during the fall. If the 1960s was the time just before Adam and Eve fell with the archangel, the current era is one where Eve acts to restore what was lost due to the fall, stepping forward as a pioneer of action. This is why the wives of blessed families have stepped forward.

Then, what should men do at this time? They must never lose to the women who are working hard. They should not live more comfortably than them. Otherwise, a time will come when they will feel ashamed. Therefore, men must take an interest in the women who are working on the front lines. Men should have the mindset that "I must move more than they do, and I must put in more effort than they do." They must achieve equality with women.

What should the Teacher do in this regard? The Teacher is also paying attention to them. Depending on their results, the future position of their husbands or families in the realm of blessing will be determined. Thus, we are entering a period of internal maintenance centered around families. You must understand this.

Let us fulfill our duties with a new heart.
When looking at all these issues comprehensively, the question is where I am going and with what disposition I am going. This is the most critical issue. Just because you have entered the Unification Church does not mean everything is fine.

Moreover, starting from the 1970s, God is placing us in an isolated position. Until now, it was a time when I was supporting you, but from now on, it will be the opposite. This is unavoidable. Until now, if you fell behind and could not keep up, I would come down and feel sorry for you, pulling you up to follow along, but that is no longer the case. It feels like a weeble wobble; if you flip it over, it feels like it keeps falling again. However, the time has changed.

Therefore, you must not have the same attitude as before. Most of those who are close to the Teacher have this attitude.

You may have experienced this, but the Teacher can sense who is approaching just by the sound of their footsteps. Those who dislike the Teacher give off a negative vibe, while those who like the Teacher emit a positive vibe.

This is a rather urgent time. What we thought we should not do when we started this path of purpose is gradually becoming the reality. Therefore, it is now time for our Unification Church to establish order and proceed strictly. When God connects the Teacher with unique individuals in the spirit world, it indicates that the time is quite busy.

Knowing this, you must diligently follow the calling you have received. Your entry into the Unification Church is due to the merits of your ancestors. Our Unification Church is not a place anyone can enter. Moreover, God does not like the Teacher to meet just anyone. Until now, the Teacher has been reluctant to meet just anyone, and that will continue in the future. You must understand that this is the time we are in.

Your entry into the church itself signifies that you have received a calling. However, following that calling is not easy. Just gathering here at the church does not mean you are following. Just as citizens of a nation have the duty to love their country, you also have obligations. In love, there must be new achievements before the nation.

Love requires conditions of relative achievement. What does this mean? It means the Three-Stage Team.

Those who love will want to give something. Just saying you love does not mean you will give without reason. Why do you want to give? Because giving connects you to them. This is how the purpose of creation is structured. When the subject and object give and receive, reproduction occurs. Right? When the subject and object give and receive, reproduction must occur. In other words, the results of creation must be brought forth. When those results come, it is good for both you and me.

This is a small thing, but centered on this, the purpose of the Three-Stage Team is to plant thoughts that are more pleasing than one's own essence. This is inevitable. This is the path to finding the results and ideals of the Three-Stage Team. This is the same in our faith life. The relationship between that person and me must be good.

To save people, genuinely love and put in your utmost effort.
Until now, we have shed tears and made indemnity to restore, but that will no longer be the case. The era of indemnity is passing. In other words, the Unification Church itself will no longer engage in indemnity.

From now on, those who are high-minded and think only of themselves will be taken away. Those who are arrogant will be taken away. Even this year, those who oppose our purpose, those who go against our purpose, and those who do not fulfill their promises will surely be taken away. I have not mentioned this to you, but I have already seen a few such individuals.

In light of these issues, the members of the Unification Church must now establish order and proceed. We are entering a time where we must fulfill our responsibilities as mature sons and daughters of God, so you must recognize the times well and determine your position to handle matters independently while committing to more valuable content. Only then can you develop and become people who can follow the purpose. You must understand this.

When you undertake any task, you think to yourself, "If I do this, I will benefit." When told to "go the three-year course," you think, "I must go this course to receive blessings." This mindset of "receiving" centers on yourself. Instead, the purpose should be, "During this three-year period, I must wholeheartedly meet the sons and daughters that God wants to find." However, you think, "I must go this course to be blessed." This is not right. This is already something different. The results will be different.

You must seek new sons and daughters, and you should not think of receiving blessings as your goal. Receiving blessings is something that happens after you love. However, because you want to receive blessings first, that is why it does not work.

Therefore, in going the three-year course, you must meet people, and when you meet them, you must love them with all your heart. The intention to meet and the intention to love are not for yourself. It is to save those people. When you love, you receive their cooperation, so you cannot fail. In that case, God can entrust everything to that person. Do not claim the results as yours. Such people will fall after one effort.

You must not seek to receive rewards first. If there are twelve brothers, do not try to be the first among them to receive a reward. Do you understand what I mean? Do not try to stand in a position of joy by receiving a reward first; instead, stand in a position of joy by receiving a reward later. Among the twelve brothers, if the first eleven receive rewards...
what should I do? Should I cry? That should not be the case. Whenever those brothers receive awards, I should think, ‘They are receiving the award on my behalf.’ I should believe that because I have put in effort and dedication before God, my brothers have received those awards. The fact that all eleven brothers received awards means that I contributed and worked hard behind the scenes, and I should feel good about that.

After that, when I receive an award myself, how should I think? I should think, ‘This award is not mine. It represents the twelve people.’ If I think this way, since a person is a spiritual being, even if I receive an award, I cannot harbor resentment. Everyone will be happy.

The Crossroads of Good and Evil
Where does good and evil begin? It does not begin elsewhere. Good and evil are two paths, and where do these two paths begin? They begin within the heart and body. In other words, they unfold as two paths within myself. Following the body is evil, while following the heart is good.

So, what do the heart and body center around? When a family has parents and three siblings living in one room, on a cold day, the body says, ‘Ah, it’s cold, so I should go sleep where my parents are.’ However, the heart opposes the body. If there is food, the body wants to eat the good food before the parents. The hands go first. But here, the heart applies the brakes.

What happens if the body does whatever it wants? If the body does what it wants, it loses the parents and loses all the siblings. Try it. If you eat whatever you want, you will soon find everyone drifting away. What does drifting away mean? It means gradually disappearing. All people will leave. In the end, even the wife you love will leave. A person who lives only for themselves will find that even their wife will leave them. At first, the heart will leave, and then the body will follow. It is bound to escape. Ultimately, the family members who were supposed to live together will all drift away, leaving one in loneliness. When this happens, one is doomed. Living solely for oneself leads to ruin.

However, the heart says, ‘Hey, you are the youngest, so you must sleep here in the cold.’ In such cases, if the heart acts according to its will for a month, two months, or three months, the parents will say to the siblings, ‘Hey, your younger sibling is sleeping in the cold, and you are all sleeping in warmth?’ and will side with the younger one. It may seem lonely, but in the end, the side will grow larger.

What happens when one’s side grows larger? If the entire family of five becomes one’s side, what happens? Everyone will cling to oneself. When they cling together, they grow. God intends to establish such a person as a central being.

According to the Calling
A person who goes all the way for good, no matter how lonely they become or how much they dislike clinging together, will have people follow and cling to them. They will not try to expel or replace that person but will instead want to establish them in a central position. When that happens, they become a central figure. A person who sacrifices for good until the end will inevitably become a central figure. Not only a central figure but also a subject and a master. Moreover, people will want to receive guidance from that person. Even in difficulties, they will discuss everything with that person and try to act according to what that person thinks is good.

Thus, a person who goes all the way for good is not rejected by their environment; rather, people gather around them. Even if they find themselves in an unfavorable position, it does not mean they are doomed. Because of those unfavorable conditions, a motive that can lead to complete unity arises, and that person naturally becomes a central figure. This is not forced but happens because many people desire it. Furthermore, since everyone wants to serve that person as a subject who becomes the master, they naturally become a central figure.

In this way, the path for good determines the position of being a center and a master, while the path for evil leads to isolation. From the position of a master, one becomes isolated from the position of a servant, and thus one is bound to perish. Everyone should understand this.

We are always engaged in such a struggle centered around the ‘I’ body. You are fighting this struggle. Therefore, when walking the path of faith, if you elevate yourself, you will inevitably fail.

Love Your Enemies
In dealing with people, there are some who have no achievements but are treated well. Such people are treated well because of the merits of their ancestors. Seeing this, our Unification Church members might misunderstand. They might think, ‘That person is new, but the teacher treats them well,’ and oppose it. But does that mean the teacher is wrong? It is not wrong. The teacher has the ability to see people. Just because God teaches in this way does not mean everything is resolved. There is still a path that one must walk.

What God teaches is a reserved subjectivity. When He told Adam and Eve to ‘have dominion over all things,’ that was also a reserved subjectivity. To enter into practical subjectivity within the realm of reserved subjectivity, one must go through the path of indemnity. It is absolutely necessary to pay the price through bloody struggles. There is no forgiveness on the path of faith. Therefore, you must walk the path of goodness.

The reason such problems arise is because of the Fall. If there had been no Fall, such problems would not occur. In other words, if there had been no Fall, the body and heart would be united, and there would be no conflict. However, because humans have fallen, they go through the process of struggle. The path of faith is influenced by these boundaries, so you must have a correct mindset and be able to criticize.

If you have wrongly criticized someone, when you see that person, your head will bow. This is unavoidable. No matter how much you are among family, when you have criticized wrongly, your head will bow.

You must seek out those standards in your daily life, knowing all sorts of things. What is the most frightening thing in daily life? It is human relationships. People are the most frightening. People are scarier than Satan. Even among our Unification Church members, what is the most frightening? It is the human heart.

I have told Chairman Yoo that the teacher has been staying up all night dealing with people to love everyone. One cannot take responsibility for the restoration history by hating people. One must love both the wicked and the good. What does this mean? Why must one love everyone? Because if one does not love everyone, one cannot represent God. The Fall is a fall into a position that opposes God’s world. In other words, the Fall is falling into a position that declares this world to be bad. Then what happens to God’s position? If God also declares this world to be bad, then He is not God. God cannot carry out the restoration history. Isn’t that so? God created this world and said it was good; if He were to come down to a position that declares this world to be bad, then He would not be God. Therefore, it is a principle to treat bad things well. One must treat bad things well.

That is why Jesus said, ‘Love your enemies.’ To love your enemies means to stand in a position where there are no enemies. To stand in a position where there are no enemies means to return to the original world, the original position, where one has not encountered the realm of the Fall in the Garden of Eden. We are fighting centered on this. Everyone is fighting to become that way.

Therefore, when you first deal with a person, even if they are a bad person, do not see them as bad. The teacher has had very good experiences even while being in prison. He has slept in the same room with death row inmates. To the world, those people seem terrifying. Isn’t that so? From the world’s perspective, they are very frightening people.

So how do you see such a death row inmate? Do you see them as a death row inmate, or do you see them as a brother when you are in the same room? Can you share the food you eat with them and eat the food they eat? You must reach that level. Ultimately, this becomes a good opportunity and condition to determine the content that can stand on a principled standard centered on God in faith and character.

When considering such issues, it is said that people are the most frightening. Satan deals with evil issues, while God deals only with good issues. Therefore, one cannot be good and evil, nor can one be attached here and there. Only people can do that.

Live for Others
In light of these issues, you should avoid being disheartened on the path of faith as much as possible. Being disheartened brings many losses. If you become disheartened, no matter how big and good your dreams are, God will distance Himself from you.

Knowing this, you must proceed with discernment in your calling. If you do not understand this, you must always pray and dedicate yourself. If you are in a sincere and humble position and say, ‘Please guide me,’ there is nothing that cannot be done. When you do that, you will come to the right time and stand in a position where you can stand. If you cannot do that, you will unknowingly find yourself in a position of indemnity.

To seek the nation

Dear everyone! I believe there are many who have come to Korea for the first time, and I hope that through this opportunity, you will study as much as possible about Korea and return.

The title I want to talk about now is "To Seek the Nation." I will discuss this topic.

The first purpose of God's providence

In this world, there are currently numerous countries. There are more than a hundred nations centered around hundreds of ethnic groups scattered across the globe. However, when we think about whether there is a nation that is truly loved by God among those countries, we find that there are none.

All the nations on Earth are not the nations that God desires; they are only those that do not align with God's will and are contrary to it. There is not a single nation that God desires. The existence of such nations is a result of the fall. This is not the form that God originally intended. Therefore, it is essential to deny this fallen world and recreate a new nation of God, which has been the purpose of God's providence for the past 6,000 years.

To seek that nation, there must be a people that can be sought. To form that people, there must be a clan that can do so. Based on that clan, a nation must be organized, and after organizing the nation, a sovereign state must be sought. This is the highest purpose of God's providence.

In this way, a clan cannot exist without a family. That family must fulfill the relationship of one husband and one wife, which is what God desires. When we think about this, we see that God's purpose for thousands of years has been to find a great nation, but the foundation of that is to manifest one couple that God desires on this earth. 

To achieve this first purpose, God has been working through providence until now. To carry this out, God has gone through thousands of years of historical processes, enduring hardships, and has found the Israelite people. To organize the Israelite people, there must be someone who stands absolutely on God's side, who can believe only in God, and who can create a foundation of complete victory without leaving any conditions for accusation within the realm of Satan. Jacob was established in such a position.

God made a new start based on the foundation of Jacob's victory over the archangel at the Jabbok River. Thus, Jacob became Israel, which means "he has prevailed." The providence began with that one person.

Centered on that one person, families were organized, and based on those families, the Israelite clans were formed, and the Israelite nation was organized, taking 4,000 years of providential process to establish the Israelite state. There had to be one person who would bring the authority of sovereignty, and that person sent to establish a global sovereign was the Messiah, Jesus.

What God desires is to establish Jesus as the sovereign of the nation and create a starting point for spreading that sovereignty across all nations. That was God's purpose in sending Jesus to the earth. However, because the Israelite people did not welcome Jesus and caused him to be crucified, all the efforts made until then were completely destroyed. If Jesus had not been crucified, a nation would have been established based on Christianity, uniting spirit and flesh on the earth, but because of the crucifixion, that standard was completely lost. Thus, it became necessary to start anew based on a spiritual standard.

Issues to be resolved in the time of the Second Coming

The history of Christianity over the past 2,000 years has developed from the spiritual individual standard to the family standard, clan standard, national standard, and world standard. In this way, the one who comes to the earth inheriting the content of that spiritual standard is the Lord of the Second Coming. However, when the Lord of the Second Coming comes to the earth, even if the spiritual national authority and the world national authority are established around democratic national authority, there is no foundation centered on any specific nation. While many Christians around the world believe in Christianity as their national religion, there are many such nations, but none of the church fathers or leaders that Christians believe in are the sovereigns of those nations. Politics is centered on political systems, and Christianity is centered on Christianity, with religion and politics separated, continuing through historical processes, but no one standing on God's side has been the sovereign of those nations until now. Therefore, this proves that a nation centered on God has not yet been established on earth.

In the end times of the world, the Lord of the Second Coming will recognize a specific nation on earth, but he must not stand on the foundation established on earth; he must create a new substantial foundation centered on the spiritual world. This is the path that the Lord of the Second Coming must take. No matter how much the national standard has been passed in the spiritual realm, without a substantial earthly foundation, the standard of completion of spirit and flesh cannot be achieved.

In this sense, it is not a problem that there are many members in the world. In any nation, even if half of the people become members of the Unification Church, it does not matter. What must be prioritized over the number of members is the establishment of a sovereign nation on earth. That is the issue.

Looking at the history of Christianity until now, many Christians have been massacred. They have walked the path of martyrdom. This is because there has not been a strong sovereign nation centered on Christianity. If there had been a nation that could respond confidently against any opposing nation, Christians would not have had to endure such persecution or the path of martyrdom until now. They have walked the miserable path of martyrdom because there has been no nation to protect them.

Considering this, if a sovereign nation is not established during the time of the Second Coming, the believers in the Lord of the Second Coming will not be able to resist such persecution. When many nations of the satanic world persecute, there must be a heavenly nation that can confront and attack. Without that, believers in the Lord of the Second Coming will face persecution wherever they go.

To prepare for that, to protect it, and to advance globally against it, a nation is essential. From this perspective, considering Korea, our Unification Church has continuously faced persecution. The path of persecution still remains. We have gone through decades of struggle to push through and rise above that opposition.

There have been countless miserable histories during that time. Now, we are fortunate to have entered an era of democracy, where freedom of religion and assembly is guaranteed; otherwise, the members of the Unification Church would not be here on earth anymore.

God has sought a sovereignty where free actions and activities can take place in a free environment, and that external environment is the democratic nation. In this realm, regardless of the sacrifices made, if we do not restore one nation to God's side, we will always have to fight from a disadvantageous position in future global operations. If we have national sovereignty, that will not be the case. On God's side, we can establish a standard of diplomatic authority and conduct God's work on an equal basis with any nation.

Therefore, the question is how to restore one nation to God's side. That is the important issue. When we think about this, if that nation is established, the democratic national authority is within the Christian cultural realm, so it will connect directly. Thus, it can be digested. Ultimately, we must restore one nation. In this regard, the organization that moves with such a mission in this world is not the traditional Christianity but our Unification Church.

Hopes for the Japanese members

We must once again reflect on how significant our mission is. In Korea, our Unification Church has fought centered on individuals. We have fought centered on families. We have also fought centered on clans and nations. Now, we have reached a stage where we can achieve a balance of power over the entire nation.

At this time, if one nation is restored to God, the question of which nation will become the second nation centered on that nation becomes an important issue in history. When the first nation is restored, what kind of people will the second nation be? If the second nation becomes one with the neighboring nations that were in relative relation to the first nation, it will be a new movement that has never existed in history.
Even if we center around Jesus and the nation of Israel, we have not been able to unite. If two different nations become one centered around a state, this would be an unprecedented event in history. We are now looking at that and believing in it. Therefore, when we think about Japan, the members of the Unification Church in Japan are not Japanese, even though they are in Japan. You all have a path of persecution ahead of you. In other words, realistically, Japan must take the underground path. When we think like that, we cannot help but rely on God and think about the path of national restoration. Our Unification thought is not about one people, one nationalism. It is globalism.

For the current Japanese people, the Communist Party is a problem because it is socialist. What if the Unification Church had a foundation greater than the Communist Party? First of all, we cannot avoid being in opposition to the Japanese people. If the Communist Party is expelled from Japan, it will raise the flag of opposition against the Unification Church, which has become globalized on a worldwide scale. In such a case, if the Unification members are few, they will suffer at once. We must think about that. However, if before such a time comes, there is one country or two countries in Asia that can resist even if the Japanese state opposes the Unification Church in Japan, then they cannot oppose it. No matter how much they oppose domestically, if there is a national standard that can resist fairly, we can defend against domestic persecution. When we think about these things, what we most desire for the Unification members in Japan is to restore one nation. This is the most significant issue.

Looking at the situation in Asia and the current situation in Japan, restoring Japan centered around our Unification Church members is numerically insufficient. Restoring the entire population of 100 million is very difficult. We must pay the price of corresponding persecution. When we think about this, we must say that Korea is the fastest. Korea is the fastest. However, when we think about it centered around Korea, Korea itself is not the nation of the Unification Church.

If we do not subdue Cain's side, complete restoration will not happen. Nearly 40 million people in Korea are not on the side of the Unification Church. Until now, they have all opposed it. We have fought to turn such a nation back in the opposite direction to make it our side. So far, we have quietly risen. Types of Time
When we consider the concept of 'time,' we can think of various types of time: the time of heavenly fortune, the time of individual fortune, the time of national fortune, and so on.
However, that 'time' does not come with a warning for individuals, families, ethnic groups, nations, or the world. That time always comes, but it flows continuously; in other words, yesterday's succession is today, and today's succession is tomorrow, which makes it difficult for us to recognize the clear turning points of that time. 

It is hard to know whether that time will be morning, noon, evening, or night. To align oneself with relative standards and practical foundations at that moment is an extremely difficult task. Throughout the historical process we have gone through, there have been many times of providence. There have been times for individuals, families, ethnic groups, and nations, centered around a single nation or state, but there have also been many such times when viewed in relation to numerous countries surrounding it. However, whether an ethnic group or nation has truly recognized that the time they are passing through is indeed the time they can embrace, and whether they have realized that the timing of that moment is when the fortune of heaven arrives, has not been the case. 

Most prophets make prophecies about specific times. And the time they prophesy will surely come. However, the essence of that coming is not a matter of months or days, but rather a specific moment within a day that serves as the focal point of that time. Therefore, it is extremely difficult to accurately synchronize with such a pivotal moment. 

Thus, while most of what the prophets have prophesied has been fulfilled, we must recognize that there have been very few instances where people have directly understood that time in their era and prepared to meet it from a relative position. It is only after passing that time that people reflect, saying, "Ah, spring had come then. Good fortune had come to our country. The time that someone had prophesied has passed." This manner of recalling the prophesied time after it has passed has always been the way humans have lived and the history of humanity up to now. 

From this perspective, there are also important times in your own lives. There are crucial points in life that must not be overlooked, which will come centered around a specific moment. That time will surely come and will cross over the hill. 

Knowing that time is an extremely difficult task. 

The issue is whether we can immediately discover and align ourselves with that time. In other words, can we accurately synchronize with God at that pivotal moment and stand in a decisive position before God, who has prepared that day? This is an extremely difficult matter. 

When God gives a gift to someone, it is exceedingly difficult for that person to receive it by extending both hands with sincerity at the right time. God repeatedly pushes forward the will of providence, but we must understand that it is exceedingly difficult for humans to recognize that time accurately and synchronize with providence. 

In life, the time of heaven's grace that is indispensable comes, but we often miss it and regret it because we do not recognize it. However, if there is someone who can look forward to that time and wait, pondering when it will come, making resolutions for a day or a month, then that person is wise. 

If someone realizes a few days later that the time has passed and repents before God, pledging to take responsibility, God may feel regret for that person having missed that time, but seeing that attitude, He will turn that regret around and extend that time again. A wise person is one who can make it possible for God to extend that time. 

Even if one does not know that time and lets it pass, if they can recognize it afterward and stand in a position to seek God's mercy, then even if the first time has passed, God will prepare a second time and open the way for it. We must think of God in this way. 

We must understand how much God loves us in a true sense, how much effort He has made to give us the necessary and appropriate gifts from heaven, and how much He has worked to help us. When we consider this, you may think that God does not care about me or is not interested in me, but that is a misunderstanding. God has come to us countless times, extending His hand to give us anything, but we, who should receive it, have not been able to align ourselves to receive it and express our gratitude at that moment. We must recognize that being in a position to express that gratitude is an extremely difficult issue. 

Therefore, we must always be cautious and think about when that time will come, whether it will be night or day, or whether it will be when I am walking or working. 

Human history has repeatedly missed that time. 

However, when that time comes, one should joyfully embrace it, yet there are cases where people greet it with displeasure. They should bring glory to God by welcoming that time in a good place, but instead, they miss it by receiving it in a bad place, causing God sorrow. We must reflect on how many times we have betrayed and ignored the times that heaven has prepared for us, considering various personal circumstances. 

Even looking at yourselves, there have been dozens or hundreds of times, but you have missed those times. If you do not feel ashamed of that, God will not grant such a person a new time again, nor will He prepare it for them. When thinking about this, we must recognize how careful our daily lives must be, and how each moment is a crucial time that pulls the strings of our destiny. We must feel that such times are passing through our daily hours. 

Therefore, those who have come to fulfill God's will must not live even one hour without vigilance. They cannot afford to be careless and live according to their own whims. They must always live with a sense of urgency. God moves to teach and connect us with that time through any moment, any time, and any environment. 

Unless one diligently seeks to know that time through their own sincerity or through the environment of certain people or times, it is exceedingly difficult to hit that time accurately throughout one's life. 

Important times are undoubtedly passing. Important times pass by without us knowing. We have thousands of ancestors, and those ancestors have wishes. If their wishes were not fulfilled in their lifetime, they hope that their descendants will fulfill those wishes and strive for that time to come. However, it is exceedingly difficult for the descendants to receive that time, which the ancestors have earnestly sought. 

In other words, many ancestors hope for their descendants to do well and, because they have done good deeds on this earth, God wishes to grant that time through those descendants. A path without discounts

<Words> At this time, I would like to talk briefly on the topic of ‘The Importance of Faith in Compassion.’ We must always remember that the path of faith we walk on this earth is not a solitary journey. 

When thinking about faith, the object of that faith is already not myself but God. Ultimately, the path we walk is centered on God. In other words, the relationship between the subject and the object is established between God and me, where the facts that occur from the subject affect the object, and the facts achieved by the object relate back to the subject. If this relationship is not established, I cannot become myself in harmony with the will, and the results of my actions for the will cannot contribute to the heavenly providence. 

God and humanity must have a relative relationship and be bound together. In other words, we must interact and become one. Depending on the degree of our oneness, changes will occur in our living environment. And when we perceive that the content of that change is more valuable than the past in our own lives, we feel the worth of our faith. 

When we feel that God is moving with us, faith in compassion begins. People generally become conscious through relative relationships. Of course, they may think in their minds, but most are stimulated through sensory organs and become conscious centered on relative relationships. 

In practicing faith, it is crucial how we apply the facts felt in our hearts to our relative living environments. You must understand this. If you have set a plan for a year under a certain standard of faith, saying, “I will do this,” that plan must not only relate to you but also how it relates to God. And how, through the oneness of the subject God and the object me, the results will manifest in this environment is what is fundamentally important. 

When the subject and object completely exchange, there will inevitably be a new reproduction, which is the third result. This third result manifests not only the purpose of the subject but also the purpose of the object, meaning it appears with a dual purpose. However, what appears as a result must be more valuable than the connection established between the subject and object beforehand, so that we can feel greater stimulation and greater joy. 

If, in February, we set some faith-related goals and practice them, we must not think of those goals as personal goals. Those goals must always be a common goal of the subject and object, and the results must always pursue the common value of the subject and object. This means that even if I am doing something, I am not doing it alone; God is always involved in it. I am not moving alone; God is moving with me. 

When we feel that God is moving with us, we can begin to have faith in compassion. Therefore, in our daily lives, we should not live meaninglessly. If there is a subject with consciousness, then the thoughts of that subject and my thoughts must run parallel, and my daily life process should not be a process limited to myself but should be felt as a process together with the subject. You must understand that faith in compassion begins when you stand in such a position. 

The issue is how to align my heart with God’s direction. People have hearts. And within the heart, there is a heart gate, or the mind gate. There are times when God interacts with us humans, with me or with others. Of course, God is always interacting with us, but the issue is how we can align our heart gate with the direction in which God interacts with us. This is an extremely difficult issue. 

Just as nature has spring, summer, autumn, and winter, and morning, noon, evening, and night, human personalities are not all the same. Some correspond to the spring season, some to summer, some to autumn, and some to winter. There are people who are like the morning, like the day, like the evening, and like the night. Even when looking at faces, they are all different. The reason for these various appearances is that the foundations they stand on are all different. Since humans are created from different motivations, the results of our appearances also differ according to the standards we stand on. Therefore, there are people who correspond to the spring season, summer season, autumn season, and winter season. In this way, humans always stand in positions corresponding to the seasons. 

There are also intermediate types of people who correspond to the spring and summer seasons, and those who correspond to the summer and autumn seasons. When viewed from all directions, each individual human stands in a different position. Thus, humans must always be in a position to establish relationships based on a center. So what is this center? This center can only be God. This center must be an absolute standard, so it cannot be our subjective position. 

Based on that subject, both the subject itself and the object, which is us humans, must revolve. When revolving, if God treats me with the characteristics of spring, I must also adjust my environment accordingly and match it. When I stand in such a position, I will inevitably feel the stimulation of compassion. It is not just me acting alone; heavenly fortune cooperates, and even if I do not want it, I can feel that the environment is naturally being created. At that time, it will definitely become a sense of compassion, and you must understand this. 

What should a believer be careful about? In dealing with matters, whether they are trivial or significant, one must not approach them personally. In other words, your heart must be taut. You must have a heart posture like a perfectly round ball that is fully inflated. Your heart state must be like a perfectly round ball, not deflated or distorted. If you have an anxious heart or a selfish heart centered on personal desires, then your heart will develop edges like a deformed ball. 

When this heart turns, it should be in contact with everything on a flat plane, but if edges develop...
The contact begins from the pointed end. When that happens, it does not stimulate the whole smoothly, but rather acts oppositely on the whole. The more we find ourselves in such a position, the more our conscience feels guilty, and we must think about how the standard of our conscience is gradually diminished. 

That is why a balanced mental attitude, like a perfect sphere, is always necessary. Thus, when any stimulus enters that mind, the whole heart should resonate. Just as when two sound bodies with the same natural frequency are placed, if one is struck, the other resonates with the same frequency without being touched, our hearts should also have a balanced mind that can resonate. Therefore, we must always strive to sense the spiritual waves that come from a single subject. 

For this reason, those who live a life of faith need time for meditation. It is said to meditate while envisioning good things. When meditating, one should open the door of the heart wide and round it, centering on God, so that God's nature and my nature, for those corresponding to the spring season, can completely exchange their characteristics with God, who is the subject of the spring season, and have a heart posture that can completely resonate. When we face the purpose that the self requires, centered on this resonating content, God will surely be with us. You must understand this. 

And when facing any task in a place where one does not feel such resonance, one should think like this: God is watching this work; I may not feel a direct relationship with Him, but I am in a relationship; God is already involved in this matter; God's will is embedded here; now is the moment I connect with that will. One should not think that they are doing the work alone. When looking at the work itself, there is always God's will established beforehand. Therefore, one must follow the will that has gone ahead and seek the points of alignment with that will. This can be divided into three parts. When we summarize our lives, it is like this. 

To align with the will, what should we do to seek the points of alignment with the will? One must not stand in an unprincipled position. With a pure heart, centered on that work, one must cultivate a living attitude that can completely exchange and resonate. Then, no matter how difficult the task is, that difficult task will not be a minus for me but a plus. Thus, it means that through that task, one can advance one step further than the position they have been in until now. 

Ultimately, when one feels the exchange between the subject and the object, heart and body, along with God, and moves forward regarding that task, heaven follows. When there is no such feeling, if one stands in a position to face any matter with a vivid feeling that God's will is already there, and that I am completely one with that will, then since the will has already come to that task, I become completely one with that will. However, this cannot be done with an unprincipled standard. When facing a task with a pure conscience, one gains strength through that task. When one gains strength like that, they can surely feel that God is with them. You must understand this. 

Therefore, when the motivation is felt in the heart while doing a task or facing a counterpart, one should think that since the will is here, I am going to the place of fulfilling that will. If it is a relative task, think that the task itself is motivated. Then, when I become one with that motivation and bring about a resultant position, if that is not for personal purposes but for public purposes, then through that task, one will feel a sense of fulfillment and strength. When one lives like this, they can achieve effects greater than those who do not engage in prayer life, even without praying. 

How do we generally distinguish what we face in daily life? First, dealing with objects; second, dealing with people; third, dealing with words. In other words, there is the relationship of dealing with objects, the relationship of dealing with people, and then the relationship of speaking in interpersonal relationships. Words serve as an indirect purpose, that is, for a third purpose. 

Therefore, in the relationship of dealing with objects, do not fall into the laws of heaven or God! In the relationship of dealing with people, do not fall into it either! And in the relationship of speaking, do not fall into it! This is how it goes. In the relationship of speaking, to avoid falling into what has been said, one must always stimulate action. Since words serve as the motivation for action, one must not fall into them when speaking. Thus, one must not fall into the relationship of dealing with objects, the relationship of dealing with people, and the relationship of speaking. Words must always stimulate action. This is the relationship in our daily lives. 

How should we deal with objects? 

So how do we elevate the relationship of dealing with objects? That is, how do we establish the position that we are not dealing with the fallen self but that God is the subject in dealing with it? In interpersonal relationships, how do we deal not just as ourselves but together with God? And even when speaking, how do we speak the words of heaven rather than just our own? This is the issue. What is spoken should not remain as mere words but must always be accompanied by action. This is what is related to our living sphere. 

When we deal with objects, workplace life will unfold, and when dealing with people, human relationships will unfold. In other words, moral relationships will unfold. And in the relationship of speaking, issues of action will arise. This is the condition in which we are relating within our living sphere. 

Therefore, in dealing with objects, do not violate the principle of law! In dealing with people, do not violate the law! In speaking and acting, do not violate the law! Whether dealing with objects or people... Of course, human relationships are established centered around people, but we must understand that we are establishing relationships from this position. 

Then, how should a believer deal with objects? One must deal with them publicly. When dealing publicly, if that object has worth, one should not see it merely as having worth but consider how to view it as having immense value. When considering how to see the value of that object as more valuable, even if the value of that object is insignificant, if one thinks that God is involved in it, then that value can be raised to an immense weight. When I believe that God is related to this object I love, the value of that object comes out with infinite significance. 

When one deals with objects with such a heart, that object becomes truly delightful. In your living sphere or in the world of your heart, such resonance will come to you. When one works with such a heart, the results will definitely feel more dimensional than what one was looking at alone. 

The fact that a task or object has given me a significant value in my environment means that through it, I have stood in a position where I can occupy a higher meaning of spiritual inner value. You must feel this yourself. Then, even after completing the task, you can be grateful. No matter how difficult the task is, if the value of the result appears to be hundreds or thousands of times greater than the effort I am putting in, if there is someone who feels that value in a heavenly way, then no matter how difficult that task is, it becomes an object of gratitude. 

Even when looking at oneself, if one is caught up in some difficult situation in interpersonal relationships and has to endure unspeakable hardships, one should not think that they are walking that path alone. They should think that they are walking that path together with God, who is the center of infinite value. And when one feels how great the value of participating in the path of suffering with God is, when they realize that the price of gratitude is greater than the price of suffering, then any path of suffering can also become a path of gratitude, and rather, it can become a path of glory before God. 

That is why one should not deal with objects thoughtlessly. One should think that that object brings either a plus or a minus to me. In other words, it either becomes a blessing or a curse for me. Therefore, when I deal with that object from the position of ten, does it become a value of eleven or nine? Does it bring a minus or a plus? One should think about this and strive to avoid the positions that bring a minus and establish a position that can bring a plus. 

Do not deal with things meaninglessly but deal with them centered on principles. 

When you seek out like this, you will already know in your heart what to do with any task. When facing any task or object, you will immediately know whether it will be a plus or a minus for you. In doing a task, your heart and will must become one with the subject and object, so that it becomes three points, and the original motivation, that is, the principle of God's creation, unfolds. Isn’t that so? 

Thus, when that object corresponds with the results of the subject and object, since the results of God's creation purpose are harvested, it brings forth good results as an object of God. 

The more good results you leave around you, the more the process of recreation within you expands and elevates. When you stand in such a position, the more you live like that, any object you deal with will already send you waves. When you deal with that object seriously with a balanced heart, free from selfishness, like a resonating sound body, feelings of whether it is good or bad will arise. Whether it becomes a plus for you or a minus… this is something you must always weigh. 

If there are no waves, from a public standpoint, with a heart like a round dial, when you deal with a task or an object, through the first impression or the initial feeling that comes in, you should have the feeling that this will definitely become a plus. In doing a task, it should not be done in a meaningless place, but with a heart that is sincere, like what God creates. If you do, good and bad results will definitely appear. 

Therefore, you should check how many percent of what you felt was accurate in your life. Always pay attention to how many percent of the first feeling that you felt was plus in your life is accurate. If you gradually habituate such an attitude of life, you will realize that among ten tasks, five or six will gradually increase in accuracy. This is what you need to cultivate. The accuracy will increase. On the other hand, if you do something that is deemed bad or not good and it results in a bad outcome, it is because the will is not in agreement. 

In this way, when dealing with all things around us, do not deal with them meaninglessly, but always deal with them centered on principles. You must understand that how to develop your empathetic feelings centered around the content of the principle of creation is extremely important. Therefore, this applies to how you deal with objects in your workplace as well. If you treat the company’s objects, which are public objects, carelessly, then that person is a minus to the company. If you think that object is a national object, a divine object, then you cannot treat even a single sheet of paper carelessly. 

With such a serious heart, if you seek the value and strive to connect your daily feelings from small matters to great matters, then you will never forget that God is with you in your living sphere. The more you deal with things, the more you will feel that God was with you in that task. A person who lives like this cannot get tired. 

If you wander around thoughtlessly and suffer losses, and if those losses become more significant than your current position, you will be hit and fall down. Therefore, for the development of this empathetic faith, you must always treat objects with care. You must deal with them seriously. If you do this wrong, it can create conditions that can trip you up on the entire path of faith. 

You should do the same when working. If there is someone practicing empathetic faith, they will immediately sense whether sincerity was put in or not. 

You should observe all things like this. 

When you are in a room laughing and talking, the feelings already come in. What kind of laughter is this? Is it laughter that is plus before God or minus? The feelings come in. You should develop and habituate yourself to be able to do that. Therefore, all the conditions around you that are centered around you are not meaningless. Everything appears as a material to develop and cultivate yourself.

is a path that somehow feels reassuring and fills me with hope. The reason believers become exhausted
When you encounter many people in the future, especially if you are to become a leader, you must discern their normal and abnormal standards, in other words, the standards of sadness and joy. When you look from the perspective of normal standards, when you rise, it is joy, and when you fall, it is sadness. You should already know what a normal tone of voice sounds like and how it differs when one is happy or unhappy.

You must gauge the tone of voice, intonation, and attitude to sense that there is something wrong behind the way that person speaks. By doing so, you can perceive the expressions of two people meeting just by observing them. Something is going on... It is not different. You should observe whether what you have sensed aligns with reality. When it feels aligned, it is certain that God is with you.

Today, Unification Church members are all being dragged by heaven, and when heaven departs, they become exhausted. This is because they do not understand the importance of experiential faith. Faith is the value that can bring victorious results within the sphere of life, centered on God's purpose, where the results can be better after encountering than before. When such results are found, no matter how much persecution comes, one can push through. They do not yield absolutely. Therefore, one must never do anything that could lead to retreat. What kind of damage would that cause? After retreating once, how difficult it is to correct that mistake. When one makes a mistake, it is incredibly hard to make up for it. Therefore, one should not even think about things that could lead to falling or becoming negative. Such things should not even be looked at. Moreover, one should not even approach such people.

For this reason, when one first receives grace, they tend to be very cautious around people. They do not carelessly engage with various things but only deal with simple matters. They are absolutely not allowed to engage with things that can lead to greed. They only deal with things that they have been indifferent to. If they do engage, they must not approach things that provoke greed. The same goes for words. They must not speak words that justify themselves.

In this way, you can find motivations to develop within your sphere of life.

Always rejoice and expand your experiential sensitivity
And when you leave home in the morning and return in the evening, do not come back in a negative state. When you return, you must be in a joyful position, that is, in a positive state compared to when you left in the morning. Only then will there be no discord in the home. If you return in a negative state, you will also give a negative feeling to your wife or children. That is a sin. From the standpoint of pursuing good, standing in such a position becomes a position that undermines good, which cannot bring joy before God and becomes sorrow.

Therefore, when you leave home and return, no matter how difficult your situation is, you must resolve that difficulty and return with conditions of joy. Even if there were frustrating and unpleasant things at work, you should not try to resolve them at home. You must either resolve them on the spot or compensate for them with greater conditions of joy before coming home. In this sense, things like alcohol can serve as a form of compensation.

Thus, you should have indirect methods that can reinforce this. For instance, you could intentionally bump your forehead against a utility pole to create a condition for compensation through that pain. You could pray for repentance with that compensation or buy some candy for your children, thinking of their joyful expressions and bringing that joy home. Alternatively, if you enjoy singing, you could sing an old spring or autumn song you liked to revive the joyful feelings of the past and bring that as your focus when you come home.

When you enter the house, whether you are interacting with your wife or children, you should do so with joyful expressions and hearts. Then the object will be determined. This way, you can completely overcome the sadness you experienced at work. You can prevent the environment that would lead to failure. You should maintain this attitude throughout the day. This is a strategy. You should not live your day carelessly.

The same applies to any situation. When you see a mountain, you should feel the beauty or mystery of God's creation through that mountain, realizing that God created such a wonderful relative object to make my value so precious, and when you feel joy and appreciation, you will experience a shocking stimulus. In such a place, when you fully engage, you become one, and you do not want to leave. You develop a child-like heart that wants to roll around in that space, and you can feel a parental heart as well.

You can feel such emotions even when looking at something as simple as nature. You can also easily become immersed in contemplation by focusing on flowing water.

As you expand this experiential sensitivity, you will even resonate with the joy that God felt during creation. This is better than praying without thought. Therefore, the issue is how you cultivate this experiential sensitivity in your life within the sphere of life. That is why you should always think about what kind of expression you should have when you face others. Digest everything as God's
Everything we encounter is a teaching material. If we do not have direct or indirect responses to this spiritual world, the objects we can relate to are God's creations. These creations resemble God's nature, so they contain elements of that nature, even indirectly. Therefore, if there is someone who expands their life to connect with the good elements and inner nature that we can relate to, that person will not face any obstacles or become negative.

Moreover, you know the law of indemnity. To become a central being, you must have many environments that can indemnify from a public standpoint. Otherwise, you cannot become a central being. In other words, you must give up a lot of your own resources. Giving up resources is a loss. Therefore, when I face difficulties or suffer damage, I must digest it through the law of indemnity.

When I do good, I give to the needy, but I also sincerely give to my enemies, and how wonderful this is. Therefore, no matter how much I am in a difficult situation, I do not suffer damage. Even if someone becomes an enemy, I digest and overcome it from a public standpoint. In such a situation, I do not think of the enemy as an enemy but rather see that place as a position where I can explore the deep value that can be gained from a more dualistic perspective.

Thus, no matter what path of suffering one may take, that suffering does not harm them. Even if it is a trap that could lead to destruction, it is unrelated to them, and rather, it can bring about a victorious result that Satan may oppose. Therefore, in living this life of faith, no matter how much Satan acts, one stands in a position to reconcile with God's. God can always take a position of God, even in the evil world. No matter what persecution or difficulties arise, they cannot break or destroy me. Rather, they bring about victory as materials for victory. This is similar to how God, throughout the 6,000 years of restoration history, has turned every opposition from Satan into a victorious outcome. Therefore, this is undoubtedly a path to become a child of God. You must relate this lifestyle.

When dealing with people, emotions respond more quickly than when dealing with objects. Therefore, you must study people extensively. When dealing with people, you must express yourself verbally, but just speaking is not enough. You should not say things that you cannot take responsibility for. In other words, do not say things you cannot act upon.

When we exchange in a space where we give and receive, and pursue a common goal, it must be understood that it will be realized.
When you feel this way and it becomes a reality, the relationship between the two people results in mutual affection. Friends formed in this way cannot help but go to the same spiritual realm. If you have a good friend, when that friend ascends to a higher spiritual realm, I can follow them. If I have formed a bond that allows me to maintain a relationship with them, I can also follow the realm they go to. Why is that? Because if they find it most pleasing to relate to me, they will complement my shortcomings and can determine a relative position in front of a subject that can be beneficial.

Thus, it is important to seek good teachers and good friends. If I can be close to a good teacher and exchange joy with them, I can participate in the glory that the teacher occupies, no matter how excellent they are. This is about developing such a tangible environment.

When you enter a neighborhood, dogs bark, and if you listen carelessly, the tones sound the same. The barking sounds are similar, but if you listen from the perspective of being with God, centered on the spiritual atmosphere, it sounds different in various ways. You can feel whether the barking dog belongs to a wealthy household or a poor one. The barking of a dog from a failing household feels wrong. However, the barking of a dog from a wealthy household sounds pleasant, and you become intoxicated by that sound. It feels good. When a dog barks, it can make you angry, right? Yet, even though it should sound shocking and unpleasant, it feels like a sound that is in rhythm and harmony. When you hear such a sound and take a closer look, it is undoubtedly the dog of a prosperous household.

Also, when babies cry, you can immediately tell whether the baby belongs to a prosperous household or not by listening from that habitual perspective. Just by listening, you can think, “Ah, why is that baby crying?” You can sense it. As you check whether that feeling is correct through experience, your accuracy will gradually increase. You need to enhance that sensitivity.

Good and evil are determined in daily life. Good and evil are not determined in thought. Do you understand? Good and evil are determined within the realm of life. Heaven and hell are not determined in your conceptual world but are determined on the stage of life. This is important.

When you ride a tram and look around at people, you can instantly recognize those who feel unpleasant and those who feel pleasant. The unpleasant people have lower spiritual energy than you.
