Whether in public or private, the person God hates the most is one who tries to use others in relationships. Following that, it is someone who judges everything based on their own interests. The person God loves is one who yields. What does yielding mean? It means I continually follow that person. I keep following what they want to do. If I keep following, I will eventually take that position. Ultimately, I can occupy everything about that person.

Therefore, I must always be gentle and humble, obeying, submitting, and yielding to what that person wants. Why? Because it is to completely occupy that person. It is not just about occupying a person but about occupying their entirety. Thus, in our faith world, we must deny ourselves and completely comply with the demands of the other party. This does not mean that I disappear; it is a strategy to fully occupy the other party. You must sense these things in your life.

The teacher does not do this nowadays, but in the past, I did it a lot. I would go out on the street and observe the feelings I received from passing people. When I thought, “Ah, that person is definitely like this,” I would check whether it was true or not by following up. I would ask, “You were like this, right?” It is not that the spiritual realm taught me; my heart already knows. So, when I ask, “You are this kind of person, right?” they are surprised and ask, “How do you know?” How do I know? It is undoubtedly correct. I can immediately tell who is in that room, whether they are doing good or bad, whether a good person lives there or a bad person lives there. You too must raise your antenna and develop it like that.

Therefore, the life of a discerning person who follows all the connections of the universe is the life of a believer. Do you understand what I mean?

You may be indifferent, but the teacher does not forget the impression you had when you first came in. I know the difference between the feeling of grace you had and your current state. If I feel a minus when I interact with you, it feels unpleasant.

Now, the time has passed when I can take responsibility and nurture you. It has become autumn, and I will no longer engage in the act of bringing nutrients. Can such acts be effective? However, in spring, it is possible. Spring is overflowing. Therefore, even if I share, I can bear fruit. However, autumn is the time when leaves dry up and stems wither, so if I share, both will become incomplete.

In the past, the teacher also performed many healing prayers. Just saying a word would make things happen as I spoke. However, I no longer engage in such acts. Why? Because it consumes itself. And because I need to do other things. You must understand that there are such issues.

Therefore, you must understand how necessary tangible faith is. Just praying is not enough. If you pray, you must put it into practice. Prayer is a covenant with God. Prayer is a covenant between God and humans, so it is a vow. Therefore, if you pray, you must certainly put it into practice. And there is no need to pray daily about one issue. True prayer is done once. Then, for ten years or twenty years, you must have the heart that longs to meet and seek that issue. A person who has such a heart is the most formidable person. Do you understand what I mean?

Because I have sworn and pledged before the Father, a person who can welcome that issue for ten years, or even a lifetime, with the attitude of searching for where they will meet it is someone who is going to the place where their prayer will be fulfilled. A person who goes once is wiser than someone who prays for ten years, because when they find it after ten years, they are already standing in the place where the purpose of their prayer has been fulfilled. Therefore, practice is the issue.

Where is that practice? It is not in the God of the heavenly kingdom but within our realm of life. Heaven and hell are separated within our realm of life. Heaven is established, and hell is established within our realm of life. The plus world and minus world come and go centered around your body and mind.

Looking at the people living around our church, there is not a single person living like that. They are all floating around like rootless weeds. There must be roots. Whether in speech or action, we must achieve the purpose of the four-position foundation centered on this triangular relationship. Everyone, what is the purpose of creation? It is the completion of the four-position foundation, right? The four-position foundation is universal.

When doing work, if the heart and body do not unite and become one, it is evil. If the heart and body truly unite, that is the four-position foundation. The same goes for work. The purpose is the four-position foundation. If my heart and body do not unite and become one with the work, the purpose of the four-position foundation cannot be achieved, so that work is of no use. Just because there is a supervisor or someone watching, do we work? Heaven and hell do not unfold in the air. They unfold centered around the unity of heart and body within your realm of life, based on the principles of creation.

From now on, you must study people. Can that person become a minus person, or can they become a plus person? You can tell just by looking. You can know just from the first impression. In that regard, the teacher is quick.

The teacher matched over 260 couples, more than 500 Japanese people, in Su-tak-ri within ten hours. At that time, I raised my antenna to the highest level. Do you understand? When I say it is undoubtedly so, the destined partners are bound together.

Therefore, tangible faith must be developed based on feelings within the realm of life rather than relying on cooperation from the spiritual realm. A person who can have a progressive faith process and life process without being harmed will undoubtedly have God with them. For those who have developed like that, when they are taught, it will be certain that God will come to them even if they do not want it. Do you understand?

God will leave those who only pray and do not act because it is a loss for Him. Therefore, you must understand that establishing the foundation of tangible faith within the realm of life is of utmost importance. Do you understand? “Yes.”

True People

When we think about how we cannot guarantee our past and present before Your will, how can we not humbly bow down before the purpose of Your providence that comes to us? Therefore, at this moment, Your infinite mercy, compassion, and love must remain with us. Please look upon us with Your fiery eyes and remove the bitter roots of sin that are lurking in our hearts. I earnestly hope for Your compassionate love, Father, as we have humbled ourselves.

February 11, 1971 (Friday), Mapo Church.
* This message was given at the Mapo District Headquarters, the first stop during the nighttime tour of the nine districts in Seoul.

<Word> Has it been over a year since I last came here? No, it hasn’t been that long, right? “It’s been half a year.” I feel sorry for not being able to come often despite being nearby. I sincerely thank you for allowing me to meet you all again this evening. I believe there are some who are here for the first time today.

What I want to talk about today is titled "True People," as written on the board. This is a very significant issue if it is a big problem.

People judge good and bad centered around themselves.
In this world, there is no one who lives without respecting themselves, whether they look at individuals or the whole. When speaking of good and bad, sad and happy experiences, there is no one who speaks from the perspective of a third party.

When one says something is good, who is at the center? It is oneself. Even when one says something is sad, the center is still oneself. This self always acts as the subject that determines happiness or unhappiness in one’s life. When we consider this issue, it would be good if the position of that "self" were right, but if it stands in an incorrect position and judges good and bad, then that life must inevitably be miserable.

If the position one stands in is the true position, then there is Heaven, or there is Earth, and there is some historical good that can criticize evil and has the power to eliminate what is not true. That power will act to reject what is not true and will not accept what is not true. When one is in a subjective position that judges good and bad centered around oneself, the universal power that can defend the truth will not bring peace but will act as a conflicting and opposing force.

When a person stands in a position they deem good, they do not consider whether that position is truly good in the real sense or if it is a bad position. They simply live their day centered around themselves, judging vaguely that "this is good in this case and that is bad in that case."

One must consider what position they are in. If it is a social organization in South Korea, that organization must be connected to a certain center and environment to form a social entity. When looking at South Korea, there is a center of the nation, and among the many people living across the Korean Peninsula, everyone, regardless of region or environment, must establish their position and situation.

When viewed from that center, there will be directions such as south, west, east, or north, and then there will be the question of how far one is positioned from the center. Only then can one establish a correct relationship with the subject, and that relationship can become one that is recognized by all.

When we consider humanity itself, we are also judging good and bad, or right and wrong, while living each day from a central position. When we look at this perspective, if there is a true center today, how should we judge good and bad based on that center? This is not a trivial matter.

The standard of a true person
Even if one has confidence in their subjectivity, believing they have the true appearance of a subject representing the nation, the question remains whether that can truly be a true center in South Korea. Furthermore, when viewed from a global perspective, there are many countries. Each country has its own historical background and cultural environment, and there are sovereigns in each country based on those environments. However, just because a sovereign represents a country, does that mean they are the true center of that country? We cannot simply acknowledge that.

Even when looking at individual countries, if we cannot recognize a single sovereign as the true center, the same applies when we look at the world today.

When we think about who can be a true center in our lives, we must consider whether the globally famous people we know or those who have authority in a certain academic field are truly true people. This is also a question. What is the standard, central, and valuable existence that can be deemed correct or incorrect in the realm of Heaven and Earth? This is the most serious issue.

If there are students in a school, when asked who the truest student is, that is only in the context of that school. That school has a past and a future. Can the student deemed the truest in the present represent the past? Can they be the center among the many students in the present? Furthermore, can they be the center before the many future students? This is a question that cannot be confidently answered.

If someone is recognized as a true person not only in our village but also throughout South Korea, can that person represent the past, the present, and the future? These are all interconnected questions.

So, how can one become a true subject? Anyone who can be a subject centered on today does not want to be just today. A true subject must remain unchanged not only today but also tomorrow, and there must be no conflicts or obstacles in connecting with the future. A true existence must be true in representing the present and true in representing the future. Here, "future" refers to a realm that transcends temporal limits and extends to the infinite world.

When considering these issues, we must understand where the standard of being true lies. There are billions of people living in the world today. Among those billions, there are sovereigns centered around South Korea, Japan, the United States, Germany, and so forth. Who among those sovereigns can represent all of humanity? The concept of a sovereign varies according to the national character. The historical process, cultural background, customs, and environment of that country influence the position of the sovereign. The policies or ideological directions proposed by that sovereign change with historical development. We can observe this gradual development in the historical process.

When looking at President Park of South Korea today, we see that he is in a process of gradual development in the historical context. Can we say he is a fixed center representing the whole? No. When looking at President Nixon of the United States, he is also establishing policies to adapt to the changing social circumstances, which means his policies are subject to change based on the evolving environment.

From this perspective, can we say that the President of the United States is a true person? Can he truly represent history, the 3 billion people of this world, and the billions of people in the future? Absolutely not.

Human emotions change with time and environmental shifts.
Every human desires to become a true person. If you have no pangs of conscience, you can maintain a dignified posture before anyone. You assert your position in that environment, saying, "What have I done wrong?" If you deny your position, you are fighting against the conditions that deny it. Then, is that position you assert one that history guarantees, that the times validate, and that the future can prove? That is the question.

When we consider a day, there is morning, noon, evening, and night. However, while the person remains the same, the feelings experienced in the morning, noon, evening, and night differ. Isn’t that so? 

When the sun rises in the east in the morning, the feeling of looking at that brilliant light is different from the feeling of watching the sunset in the evening. My heart and all my emotions change with the sun. Although I do not change, my feelings change according to the changes in the environment.

In the daytime, feelings differ based on the day, and in the evening, they differ based on the evening, and at night, they differ based on the night. Additionally, the feelings experienced in ordinary environments differ from those felt in scenic spots. The emotions felt at the top of a mountain, in a valley, on flat land, or in the wilderness differ.

When we consider this, the question arises as to where the roots of the subjectivity that wants to assert itself as absolute and judge good and bad are located.

A person does not suddenly become a remarkable being just by living in this era. There is always a historical aspect to it. This cannot be denied. The existence of oneself today has been formed through a historical process from the past. When considering oneself, there is always a world related to oneself, and one cannot escape that world. Furthermore, one cannot deny the world of connections.

The existence of "I" must follow the connection with parents. When viewed from the center of "I," there are relatives connected. The connection of siblings forms the bond of kinship. As that connection expands, it becomes a clan, a nation, and ultimately, the world. We must understand this.

Thus, asserting oneself is not about denying those connections and relationships but rather asserting oneself within the context of those connections. We must recognize this fact.

Therefore, the standards of assertion vary according to cultural backgrounds, and national...
the standard claimed varies depending on the position of the adversary. We can see that the perspective on good and evil also changes according to that position and environment. During the Japanese colonial period, the Communist Party could not be tolerated in Japan. There was no freedom to have political parties and promote the Communist Party in public as there is today. However, things have changed today. How have they changed? It is not that the Communist Party itself has changed, nor that the Japanese people have changed. When the political direction or environment of that time changes, the resulting content also changes. This fact cannot be denied.

When I was in school, I was friends with communists. We fought together under a common goal to overthrow the Japanese emperor's ideology. At that time, they were friends of friends and comrades among comrades who were indispensable. But why have we split now? It is because the direction and goals we face are opposed.

When this happens, you may live your life thinking, "I was born as a citizen of the Republic of Korea. I was born as a child of a certain family and am living a life that is not lacking. Conscientiously, there is nothing to feel guilty about. Isn't it right to live like this?" You should understand that saying it is right is based only on the environmental connections and content of that time, and it is said from a position unrelated to the overall environmental content.

You may say good or bad based on your daily life, but is there anyone among you who says, "I am satisfied with this. I do not want anything better than this"? There is none. There will be no one who says, "This is enough. I am fine with just this." You will seek something more valuable, happier, more precious, and something with infinite value than today.

In seeking that, you do not look for it within your living space, at home, in trivial household matters, or in the relationships with your wife and children. If someone has a broad perspective and strives to find it for the Republic of Korea, that person can still be a center that many people can look up to and can lead many people, even if they have not found it. They are in a better position than those who have not sought it, and they can assert themselves in front of any environment based on their own feelings and knowledge.

When we look at human life today, we see that people are happy and trying to be satisfied from their current position. They try to expand that to achieve happiness globally. Moreover, the global situation is increasingly entering our living space. In just about 20 minutes, we can directly feel all the events happening in the world.

Therefore, in the future path of life we must take, if we affirm that "this is good" based on the content centered on the Republic of Korea, it will not even enter the global axis. Such a time is approaching before our eyes. Thus, we must be global. They say, "Currently, the Republic of Korea is centered on economic revival and will become a developing country when it surpasses 1975." However, that is not absolute. The ultimate developed countries are determined, and from there, developing countries are formed.

True happiness

History has been developing until now. When the beliefs of individuals align, families are formed, and when the claims of families align with each other, a communal society centered around clans is formed. When the claims of clans are the same, they unite to form a nation.

However, when the claims of nations are all different, there will be no way for humanity to unite based on the world. If we look at the Republic of Korea, if we say, "What the Republic of Korea claims is the best, and everything that other countries claim is bad," then the Republic of Korea cannot unite with other countries. If the Republic of Korea combines with a more valuable counterpart, greater value will emerge, but for these two to unite, it cannot be done with claims centered only on the Republic of Korea. When the claims include content that can be better as a common goal, they will unite if it results in no loss compared to before.

We are the same. Through daily life, we interact with friends or encounter many people and events. When we meet someone and establish a relationship, it is based on the point where both of our purposes align. There is no way to establish a relationship when one party is happy and the other is sad. When we look at it this way, if our personal lives discover that the standard of mutual common purpose brings benefits beyond our current positions, we cannot separate.

From this perspective, when an individual claims to be happy, if that happiness is limited to that person alone, can it be considered true happiness? If we say that a specific person, A, is "happy," meaning that they deny everything and claim to be happy alone, that is not happiness. If that is the case, that person will be expelled by the unhappy people. They cannot exist.

Then, what should the content of happiness be? It must have a possibility for everyone, even if one is in a high position. "It should not only be you; all people can be like that. When you follow the path you take, not only you but also people in the east, west, south, and north can all be happy." When that is the case, without that person having to claim it, everyone will automatically want to unite around them.

The myriad thoughts of people

When we look at the question of what is good and what is evil, there may be people who say, "What do I care about what is good and what is evil? Such talk is for religious people." There may be people who say, "What the Unification Church's Reverend Moon says tonight is the same as what any other pastor says. The words of Christians and believers are all official statements."

Is good truly necessary for humans? Why is only good necessary and not evil? This is the issue. If you ask people who are accustomed to their living habits to raise their hands if they like to cry, they would say, "Why would you even ask that? The person asking is a bit strange." No one likes to live with a frown, saying, "Oh, I'm dying." But if you ask people to raise their hands if they like to laugh and sing, even if you tell them not to, they will raise their hands.

Then, when we look at the question of why crying is bad and laughing is good, this is a myriad of circumstances. Person A may shed tears for no reason when the chilly autumn wind blows, and the persimmons in the front yard are ripening yellow while the leaves are turning yellow with autumn colors. They may cry upon seeing the persimmon tree's leaves fall. There are people who feel sad about that and people who feel hurt and cry. Tears shed from being beaten by a husband or from some worry are not good. They do not seem good.

God has given humans a poetic emotion, asking them to think about the desolation of life when they see the persimmon tree's leaves fall. "If life ends like this, it will fall like the fallen leaves," and when a person feels the impermanence of life and sheds tears, that is vastly different from someone who is crying because they are hurt by their husband.

There are also myriad differences in crying when beaten by a husband. I shouldn't talk about this regarding women, but I mention it because women tend to cry easily. But men, do not take it lightly. Among women, there may be those who cry after being beaten by their husbands, saying, "I can't believe this. Did I come to this family to endure this? I hope that husband breaks his leg and falls apart in a few days." On the other hand, there may be those who, while being beaten, say, "How could you do this? Wouldn't your hand hurt? I'm okay, but what joy is there in treating me like this?" There are different types of tears.

For example, let's say there is a very pitiful and miserable family that has no choice but to go three days without food. How pitiful is it to live in a situation where they have not eaten for three days? There may be a son, a father, a mother, and a grandson who all feel the misery of not having food. If there are ten family members, all ten have gone three days without food, so how miserable would that be? They would feel it as the greatest misfortune. However, if that family has no hope that after three days of hunger something will change, and if it is just going to end like that, what would happen? In such a situation, they would be stunned.

They would be stunned, but even here, the nature of tears differs for each family member. The grandfather, who has accumulated a lot of virtue, might think, "In my 80 years of life, I have never known the suffering of hunger, but now that I am in a situation where I cannot eat for three days, I realize that there are such valleys in life. Wow! I have experienced a truly good lesson." Meanwhile, the grandmother might see the grandfather and think, "That old man has lost his mind. How can he sit still and daydream when we are starving to death?" Other family members would have their own different thoughts.

If you lay out ten people, there will be a global spectrum of thoughts. The hunger is the same, but the internal depth, shape, and circumstances are all different for each of the ten people. This is the myriad of circumstances. Externally, they may all be shedding tears and lamenting in despair, thinking it is the end, but some may instead find a good opportunity to taste the deep valleys of life and the profound connections of humanity. It can be a rare chance to cultivate a deep emotional flow that cannot be found in ordinary society.

However, there may also be those who, in such a situation, struggle and think of it as a foundation for curses and resentment, hating it. This is the myriad of circumstances.

Is happiness only in laughter and living?

From this perspective, what kind of people will we ordinary people become? Will we become those who say, "I don't know," and give up, or will we become those who think, "Life is fleeting, but there is something worthwhile in this life," and seek such things? Without a doubt, you would all want to be like the latter. Isn't that strange? When you see that, it feels unpleasant.

From the perspective of the dire situation you are in, it feels unpleasant. If you are on the verge of death, you should at least pretend to die, but it seems like you are indifferent, and the person next to you is stunned. However, when we look at the question of whether something is closer to truth among the bad things, there are myriad circumstances involved.

Try to statistically analyze the types of people who have been recognized by the state. When you look at those who have been recognized by the state, generally, they are not people who worked in a position where all thirty million people could say, "I can do that. I can do that. It must be me." Such people are not eligible for recognition. If everyone can do it, would everyone be recognized? Recognition is given to only one person, the best. It is not about selecting someone for recognition from a position that everyone can occupy.

When everyone betrays the state, when everyone betrays the nation and is in a state of despair, when all flee and say they do not want to be involved, it is the person who remains there, who has a central integrity, who tries to instill loyalty and a spirit of patriotism, even if their body is torn and they face hardships and suffering, that is given recognition.

When everyone has fled and disappeared, the one who remains and thinks, "I am the only one left. I will win the first prize," cannot remain. The person who has the desire, "I did this, so I will be recognized by the state," does not stay until the end. What can such a person do with an award? The award is not the issue. Such a person cannot remain. However, the one who thinks, "Even if I lose my life, I must preserve a spirit of the nation that will not disappear," loves the country more than their own life and endures with a greater patience than their own life. When the content of their practice can be recognized publicly, even if they do not want to flee, they are elected as a recipient.

Thus, the motives and content for being elected as a recipient are miserable. It is not a place where you and I can laugh and dance joyfully. It is a place where sorrow, pain, and loneliness invade and threaten one's life. The person who overcomes that environment and establishes their subjectivity will be remembered as a loyal subject representing the state and will be selected as a recipient of recognition.

This is something we can also understand in social life. True loyal subjects do not emerge in peaceful times. A true loyal subject emerges in a state of emergency, when the fate of the nation is at stake, and everyone is in an environment where they cannot take responsibility. The more historical urgency it contains, the more it is the person who takes responsibility and moves forward. No matter how evil the future, past, and present world may be, such a person will remain as a historically representative loyal subject and will remain as a center that can lead the loyal subjects of the future world.

When this happens, the state can rank loyal subjects as the first, second, third, fourth loyal subjects, and so on. In other words, a standard can be established, and grades can be set based on whether one is better or worse than that standard.

From this perspective, we can say that human happiness is not only in laughing and living. Even if we are caught in a situation of hardship that we cannot overcome as humans, if we can develop that hardship meaningfully and invest our lives to possess valuable worth that others do not have, we will be learning at a higher level from there. You must understand that ideologies and all principles are formed on such a foundation. History proves this.

Where does the better ideology come from? It comes from a better social environment.
Standing in the center does not mean coming from a place where one eats and lives well. It is about being in the midst of a better social environment but entering a more miserable position, digesting the miserable content, and overcoming it. You must understand that the motivation to innovate a lazy society and propose a revolution to a higher world in the future started from a worse position. Therefore, there has never been a true sage born in that era who was welcomed by the country and the people. Such a sage is a false sage.

What does not change and what is good
When you ask whether you will become famous in your neighborhood or in the country, you do not even need to ask; the answer is, "You should become famous in the country." If you ask, "Will you become famous in the country or globally?" the answer is that you wish to become globally famous. Among those who have come here, there may be distinguished individuals, but there are also less distinguished ones. It is not about being distinguished or not; if you look into everyone's heart, everyone wants to be a global figure. If one does not have this desire, they are not human. If someone is not human and feels bad about not being human, that is their choice... (laughter) Is there anyone who would feel bad about that?

Even a child with a runny nose would choose to be the President of the world over the President of South Korea if asked, "Do you want to be the President of South Korea or the President of the world?" Can you then say to that child, "Hey, how can you ignore the President of South Korea and aim for the President of the world? That makes you a traitor"?

So, what is a true person? You must understand that being true does not mean being in the flow of passing water. No matter how fast the water flows, it cannot wear down the edge of a rock in an instant. Water may flow for a thousand years and gradually wear down the rock until it becomes round, but it does not happen overnight.

When you are asked whether you will be flowing water or a rock, no one would say they want to be flowing water. Why is the rock good? Because it does not waver and does not change. No matter how much time passes, it remains unchanged. In this sense, what is precious and good? Once something is good, it does not flow away; it endures. Wishing for something to last forever is the true happiness that humans desire. What good is it if today is good but tomorrow is not?

Thieves may enjoy seizing gold and treasures while threatening lives for a few days, but afterward, they end up in prison. Is that good? It is not good. Something that is good once must be guaranteed to be good forever. It should not decrease tomorrow compared to today; it should increase. If you live with the feeling that next year will be better than this year, and the 70s will be better than the 60s, and the 80s will be better than the 70s, then you will be happy.

Happiness is nothing other than this. When you achieve a certain goal, you can feel happiness. In other words, when you say, "I hope this will be good," and then you achieve it, you will say, "Ah, that’s good." Those who wish to be happy when they achieve their goals must be very careful. If achieving a goal ends there, that person is already unhappy. They must set a higher goal beyond that goal and be able to say, "Let's go again." The first goal should be digested as a training purpose and used as material to run towards the second goal for tomorrow; if that is the case, that person will not know fatigue. However, if one only plans for the first goal and achieves it, what will happen next? It ends there.

The reason South Korea is corrupt is that once they seize power, they are satisfied with it and think that is the end. A nation with such a mindset cannot remain in the world.

Look at the Jewish people. The nation of Israel is a formidable nation. For 2,000 years, that nation has been scattered all over the world. Could they even think of having their own country? They have lost their country and their ethnicity, but they have a mindset that individuals can represent their nation and country. What kind of mindset is that? It is the belief that they are the chosen people. This is a formidable mindset. "The nation of Israel is the chosen people. There is an absolute God in this universe who loves our nation. The trials and pains we endure are not meant to destroy us but to test us and make us the ultimate owners of history." This is truly a formidable mindset.

The essence of truth
We, who believe in the Unification Church, use the term "tang-gam," which is the greatest word. Even when facing death, if you think, "It is tang-gam," and when going to a joyful place, if you think, "It is tang-gam," then you cannot rejoice alone even in happiness. When you are happy, you must offer a sacrifice.

In the same way, the nation of Israel is a great nation. They believed, "There is an absolute being who is the center of the universe. No matter how much Hitler targets the lives of Jews, heaven will surely grant us victory." This belief proved to be true. They were a nation that held the conviction that "even if one person remains, that blessing cannot be transferred." Even if everyone dies and only one person remains, that nation will resurrect. Even if everyone dies and only one person remains, that country will start from there.

When the remnants scattered everywhere hold hands and open their hearts, saying, "Let us go to the place we have longed for," that nation will start again. What kind of nation will that be? It will be the nation that God has desired. As a nation that can lead all people, even if there are greater trials than historical trials ahead of that nation that is to establish a peaceful kingdom, it will not be a problem.

Currently, about three million Israelites live within nearly one hundred million Arabs. However, they do not lament having lost their country and ethnicity; they have a proactive mindset that they can revive their country and reshape their ethnicity. They possess a superior mindset that is above any ideology held by any nation or people in the world. When these three unite and their numbers increase, their movement will inevitably become a global issue. That is how it is. So, were the trials and pains they experienced in the past misfortunes? No. If that misfortune became the driving force to digest future happiness, then it is not misfortune.

In this regard, we seek to find true people. We all wish to become true people. However, did the thought of wanting to become a true person start from the beginning, midway, or at the very end? We must find that out. Before I say I want to become a true person, I want to find a true person first.

Truth does not change according to regional conditions or is not subject to environmental dominance. What does that mean? What is true in Dongdaemun is not untrue in Seodaemun. Things that change according to Dongdaemun Market and Seodaemun Market are not true things. It must remain unchanged whether you go to Dongdaemun, Seodaemun, Seoul, or a mountain village. People like pure gold. Do you like pure gold? Do you like gold nuggets? Among gold, people prefer pure gold. Why do they like pure gold? Because it possesses a transcendent value that is not subject to environmental dominance. It exists in a transcendent position that is not governed by the environments of the past, present, or future. It is the same in the past, present, and future. Whether seen by a sad person or a happy person, it is the same light. It does not change day or night.

When you delve into the essence of truth, the first thing is that it must not change. It must not change. Treasures do not change. When comparing synthetic diamonds and real diamonds, synthetic diamonds may not show any flaws initially and may even be more popular at first. However, they can change color and shape over time. But real diamonds do not. They possess a transcendent quality that is not subject to environmental conditions.

Thus, when probing the essence of truth, it must first be unchanging. Furthermore, truth must have not only immutability but also eternity. It must possess both immutability and eternity. Additionally, it must have uniqueness. In other words, it must be absolute. What does it mean to be absolute? It means it is the only subject. To be the only subject means it can be the source of all comparisons. In other words, it is the decisive position to judge what is right and wrong. You must understand that. Right? Pure gold is the standard; how much pure gold is there in fake gold? Isn’t that right? It is not two but one that possesses that position.

The original measure (原器) is found only in the French Bureau of Weights and Measures. No matter how many countries in the world create their own tools for measuring length or distance and boast about them, if they are measured against the original meter, even a thousandth or ten-thousandth of a difference makes it fake, right? Even a billionth of a difference makes it fake. You might think that is acceptable, but if you strictly examine it, even a difference of several tens of billions makes it fake.

In this light, the question of whether there are indeed true humans is a significant issue. Isn’t it? There are great figures in South Korea. Who do you consider a great figure in South Korea? Great figures, sages, and true people

The sage advocates, but the person who advocates is not the center.
No, that's not it. This is different.

"It is centered on Heaven." This is what makes it different. You must understand this.

Happiness cannot exist apart from emotions.

Now, as the presidential election day approaches, the ruling and opposition parties boast about who is better, right? So, who is better? Who can determine who is better among those who claim to be better? If someone who does not know judges who is better, is that a real judgment or a fake judgment? It is a serious issue. If humans decide who is better among themselves, the person determined to be the best will complain about the next person. "What, in terms of height or ability, is worse than me?" They can complain. This creates factions. Considering such issues, humans will keep wrestling with each other without resolution. This is the situation that will unfold. 
Then, who will make this decision? If two people who claim to be better cannot decide, can someone who is not in that position make a decision? No. Therefore, humans cannot make decisions among themselves. In other words, decisions made among humans cannot be trusted. 
If there is a subject who is superior and transcendent, who can conform to the past, present, and future, and can recognize and certify that environment, people will seek the judgment of that subject. This is how it works. Who would that subject be? If it is God, who created heaven and earth, then no one else can appear. That person appears as the absolute God. 
When that absolute God feels and makes a judgment, it becomes absolute. When that happens, a new order can be established in the human world. Without that, we cannot establish order; this is the conclusion of our theoretical pursuit. 
If there is an absolute being and someone who has been judged to be right by that absolute being, will humans follow the absolute being or the one judged to be right by the absolute being? Who would you follow? Please answer. This is a serious issue. If you think about it, you would want to follow the absolute being. That is the conclusion. Therefore, in the human world, we seek to transcend humanity and pursue God. We are envisioning the highest happiness that our conscience desires. Ultimately, the one who cannot be absent is God. Only God can be the absolute standard, and only God can bring the conditions for our happiness, so we say we will center on God. Thus, the thought of religion has never departed from the beginning of human history. This means it should not start centered on humanity. In other words, truth cannot start centered on humanity. 
So where should truth begin? It must begin from the absolute God. It should center on the absolute God and present the contents of human ethics based on heavenly ethics, where heavenly ethics and human ethics can meet, and where God can be pleased and we humans can be pleased—our happiness aligns with heaven. When we find that meeting point, human happiness and God's happiness become one. Only when heavenly ethics and human ethics unite, and heavenly affection and human affection unite, can everything be determined. 
In this regard, humans stand in a position where they cannot help but pursue the absolute God centered on religion. Therefore, true sages have introduced God. Do you understand? They did not introduce themselves. Humans should not come forward while pushing God behind. They must introduce God. That is why sages could not help but say, "The absolute being is like this." 
So, among the sages, who has most accurately uncovered God? Jesus, who seems to know nothing, said, "God is my Father." That is a very good conclusion. When we consider where humans can stay at the highest point before the highest absolute being, the best position we can pursue before the absolute God is, "You are my Father, and I am your son." There is no higher position to be found. The conclusion has been reached. That one statement of Jesus represents the enlightened authority of humanity. When he says, "You are my Father," if there is a response from the other side, "Yes!" then everything in the world will be resolved. If the absolute being becomes only the father-in-law, the world will be in turmoil, but he is the son. 
What is the privilege of the son? It cannot be severed. Can it be severed?
cannot be severed. Whether it be a blade or power, nothing can sever the bond of a son. From the day one says, 'That kid is not my son,' the father's heart will never heal from that pain. No matter how much power or ability a father has, the relationship with his child cannot be severed. Can it be severed? It cannot. Not even the power of a nation or God can sever it. This is absolute.

This is what Jesus proclaimed. He was not satisfied with just saying, 'God is my Father.' Anyone can say that. He added, 'I am the only begotten Son of God.' What does it mean to be the only begotten Son? It means that in terms of emotional connection, there is no one but Jesus. The essence of the heavenly principle and heavenly love is contained in that one statement.

Through the heavenly principle, God and Jesus are in a father-son relationship, and through heavenly love, God and Jesus are in a relationship of paternal love. Because they were willing to give their lives to establish such a relationship, Christianity inevitably became a truly global religion. If that were not the case, it would lead to the conclusion that God does not exist. Because God exists, the democratic world is nurtured within the Christian cultural sphere, and from that foundation, a new world will extend. This connects to the idea of the Second Coming, doesn't it?

True People
If I were to ask you, 'Would you like to be the son-in-law of the President of the Republic of Korea or his son?' you would say you want to be his son. If I asked, 'Would you like to be the son-in-law of the world president or an adopted son?' you would want to be an adopted son even if it means being less than a son. Furthermore, if I asked if you would like to be a son, that would go without saying. This is how it goes up. The human heart seeks the highest point. Everyone wants to be number one in the world and has the desire to make heaven and earth their own. Humans possess the potential to achieve as much as they can. How great is your heart? It is so great that even if God were to put in ten or a hundred, there would still be room left. This is how wonderful humans are.

Do women want to be daughters of God or daughters-in-law of God? They would say, 'I want to be a daughter.' Regardless of whether they are beautiful or not, if they are God's daughters, that is certain, right? Even if their eyes are small, if they are daughters, that is not something that can be questioned. Whether one is beautiful or not is not the issue. The issue is whether one is a daughter or not. This is why Jesus said, 'God is my Father, and I am the only begotten Son.'

However, if there were only God and Jesus, it would be lonely, and a nation could not emerge from that. If only the men whom God loves are chosen, the world cannot emerge. If only men exist, they will die within a hundred years, and that is that. It cannot be done. Therefore, daughters of God are needed. This is why there is a need for daughters. This is why Jesus said, 'I am the bridegroom, and you are the brides.'

In the midst of an evil world, coming as the Son of God and becoming the only begotten Son who can possess God's love, centered on the infinite value, we seek one daughter who can discern the evil world and unite with it. This is why He said, 'I am the bridegroom, and you are the brides.' The Son of God is universal. He is not petty. Because He is universal, He leads the global stage and seeks to hold a unique global feast that has never been seen before in history. The day when the sons and daughters of God can hold a feast centered on the son and daughter-in-law is the day that humanity hopes for, and it is the path that fallen humans seek. This is the idea of the Second Coming in Christianity. It is the feast of the Lamb. Do you know what the feast of the Lamb is? It is the feast of the bride and bridegroom.

Not only that, but those who believe in Jesus become the bride and bridegroom, but I am the elder brother, and you are the younger siblings. We are brothers. Ultimately, it is through the cooperation of God and humanity that the foundation of an ideal family is established. This is the mainstream thought of Christianity.

The True Person is One Who Has Occupied God
So, what kind of person is a true person? A true person is one who has completely occupied the one and only God. Since God is the absolute being, if one can completely occupy God, one cannot become the absolute being, but one can become a relative absolute being. This means that while one cannot become a male God, one can become a female God. (Laughter)

Although God is the absolute being, can God be without a counterpart? No matter how high, would it be fun to be alone? It would be boring to be alone. Even if one has the whole world, if one is alone and laughing, would that be considered normal? What would God think about that? Would He say, 'He is crazy'? We should not say that He is crazy, but indeed, He is somewhat crazy. If the world's number one president is sitting alone in a room and laughing with no one around, what would people say? They would say he is crazy. The same goes for God. However, if a little servant looks at a piece of paper and giggles, that is not a problem. If there is a counterpart, one can determine infinite value. Without a counterpart, there is nothing at all. God also needs a counterpart, right? But who is the counterpart that God needs? It is only humanity.

So what does God want to do with humanity as a counterpart? Does He just want to look? What does He want to do? He wants to live together. How does He want to live? Does He want to live fighting? No. He wants to live in love. In this way, God becomes the Father, and I become the Son.

From this perspective, what is a true person? A true person is one who has completely occupied God throughout history. People like Confucius, Buddha, and Jesus also tried to occupy God but died without doing so. They tried to express the content but could not practice it. When one reaches a position where they can practice and say, 'This is it,' that is when they become a true person.

So, if one completely occupies God, is that the end? No. One must not only occupy God but also completely occupy the one and only love that exists within God. After that, one must bind recognition and heavenly love within oneself. Only such a person can become a true human being.

However, if one follows someone who has been judged as a true person by humans, can they occupy God and possess God's love? No, they cannot. One must be someone who can go beyond that person to occupy God and possess God's love to be a true person.

So what do Unification Church members want to do? Do they want to become great people or saints? When you are asked, do you want to be a saint or a great person? "I want to be a saint." Did Jesus fulfill His purpose or not? Did Confucius fulfill his purpose or not? Did Buddha fulfill his purpose or not? They all hoped to achieve this, but they could not. The ultimate goal of these individuals who sought to fulfill their purpose is for God and humanity to become completely one. They needed to reach that position, but did they find such a position? They did not. Jesus also worked hard for 2,000 years to find that.

So, should we be worse than Jesus or better than Jesus? If Jesus planted a seed and looked at the harvested grain, and said, 'You are not as good-looking as I am,' then that would mean Jesus would also fail. Even if one planted a single grain of inferior quality, when it is harvested, it is hoped that it will be a perfect yield. Isn't that the wish of the one who planted the seed? Similarly, if Christianity has been spread globally, the results of the people produced through Christianity must not be inferior to Jesus. The conclusion is that they must not be worse than Him.

So what must be done? One must acknowledge God as their Father and become a son or daughter of God, someone who can receive God's love, someone whom God cannot help but love. By doing so, one should not only live for the Republic of Korea or the nation of Israel but become someone who can love the world as if it were their own country. This is how one becomes a person better than Jesus. The conclusion is simple.

The Relationship with God in Daily Life
Jesus died in the process of fighting to fulfill His purpose through the nation of Judea towards Rome. Now, the world has become a stage, and since we are within the realm of democratic life, when good content is decisively revealed, the world can be embraced in one fold. In such times, becoming the sons and daughters of God and receiving all of God's love, we must establish families that can make God happy and embrace the world.

This transcends all races and surpasses all borders and socio-cultural backgrounds, aiming to establish a new cultural world. In other words, not only the currently developing cultural processes but also the highest culture, the resulting culture, must be viewed while living in a way that harmonizes heaven and earth around a supreme standard.

When that happens, God will not be the distant God that we think of conceptually, but rather the God who directly accompanies us within our living sphere. As recognition and heavenly love, and heavenly love and recognition, when we can have a love relationship that is equal and reciprocal, not a vertical relationship, that is when true humanity is determined, and a family is formed centered around true humanity.

However, there is one problem here. What does this mean? It means that a vertical relationship is a hierarchical relationship. This alone is not enough. Does a father wish for his son to be unsuccessful or successful? Answer me. If a father truly loves his child, does he feel bad if his son is better than him, or does he want his son to be better than him? "I want him to be better." He wants him to be better.

Imagine walking down the street and seeing an old, unattractive man holding his son. If the son is not particularly handsome and resembles his father, and someone says, 'That kid is much better looking than his father, a million times better,' the father would feel good about that. If that is the case, does it not imply that the father is a million times less good-looking? Yet the father is still happy. Who does that child resemble?

When we look at the relationship between God and humanity, if God is the father of humanity and humanity is the son of God, would God feel good or bad if humanity is said to be better looking than Him? (Laughter) If it is bad, then it means God is not as good as humanity. (Laughter) Surely, God cannot help but feel good about it, right? This is why love is necessary.

Do you want to be better than God or not? Answer me. "I want to be better." (Laughter) If you say too much, it might be rude. I apologize, but there is a desire to be better.

In ancient East Asia, people would greet their fathers every morning and evening. However, if a son thinks, 'I wish I could be a father once, and I wish my father could be like me once,' how would that be? 'Does that mean the father is always above and I am always below?' That is a thought that could arise. Isn't that so? While a hierarchical relationship is good, if it is always that way, it is unpleasant. It is fine if there is a time when one can also be a father. However, if the father is always in the upper position and the son is always in the lower position, it feels bad. Do you not feel that way? That is a possibility.

The father-son relationship is hierarchical in terms of position. Therefore, when the son asks the father, 'Father, let me have your position. I want to see what it is like to be in your place,' and the father says, 'Hey, you cannot do that,' then it means it cannot be done. God, as the absolute being, must consider that as well.

Thus, the question of what position humanity will be placed in cannot be a trivial matter from God's perspective. Therefore, what position did God want to place humanity in? In terms of position, it is a hierarchical relationship, but in terms of living, it is a relationship of mutual respect and reciprocity. This is the issue that must be pursued to understand where God should be.

Where Should God Be Respected?
So, if it is to be a relationship of mutual respect, where should God be? God is an incorporeal spirit; in what position should He be with humans? He should not always be above, right? If He is only above, then He must be in a father-son relationship.

From the perspective of humanity, God is the most precious being. He is the only one, the most precious being, so where should we hide this precious being? If there is only one treasure, and if it can be taken away, it has a value that could cause the world to collapse. Where should it be hidden? Can we feel secure putting it in a safe? When you watch spy movies, they often break into safes, right? There is always a possibility of stealing that too. Isn't that so? If that is taken away, the whole world would be in chaos, and it would be easy to steal. If that is the case, would you keep it in your wallet or in your room? There is no place to put it. Even if you bury it in the ground, someone could steal it. You cannot put it inside your body or in your bones either. In that case, it could be taken away while you sleep.

So, where should we keep the most precious and good being? What should we do? People might think, 'I wish it would not be visible to ordinary people, but only to me.' If one discovers that, it is the greatest discovery. Is there any other way? Wanting it to be invisible to ordinary people but visible only to oneself means wanting it to be known only to oneself.

Therefore, when it comes to where to keep God, do we want to carry that good and precious being with us all the time, or do we want to keep it at a distance? Even mothers cannot help but leave their babies behind, but they always want to carry them with them, right? If there are no people around, they want to kiss their babies on the cheek all the time. They do not want to be apart.

How much more so would it be to keep such a precious God up in the highest heaven? Would that be pleasing? No, it would not. We want to carry Him with us all the time. Therefore, when we ask where we want to keep God, since He is invisible, we want to keep Him in a place that only we can know. Is there such a place in our hearts and bodies? Yes, there is. That is the heart. It means placing God in the center of our hearts. Then who can take Him away? So, did God do well to be invisible or not? (Laughter) He did well to be invisible. If God were visible, we would say, 'He is over there, and over there too…' and that would make Him worthless. Because He is invisible, He has value. It is something that only I know.

God thought of this, which is why He has always been invisible. Did He do well to be invisible or not? (Laughter) He did well to be invisible. If God were visible now, what would happen? Thieves would invade every day. Think about it. Today, America and Russia are fighting fiercely over land; if the one who created heaven and earth were sitting there, would they engage in a nuclear war to make Him their own?
What is seen here can lead to great trouble. That is why God could not be visible for the sake of world peace; did He do well or not? God is invisible because He knows all of this. 

Although God has a hierarchical relationship with me, He has an internal and external relationship with me, so who can take away the God that is within me? Even if you kill me, you cannot take Him away. Even in death, the heart remains. 

An 80-year-old man may have a heart like that of a 16-year-old youth. This elder is the same, right? "Yes." Even elderly men with gray hair would want to marry a 15-year-old girl if they had the chance. (Laughter) That's how it is. What is there to dislike? The heart is all the same. The heart does not age. Therefore, it is eternally youthful, eternally adolescent, eternally spring-like, and it has an absolute standard that can be filled with hope in our human hearts. 

The heart is vast. The heart can make South Korea prosperous, but it does not end there; it also wants to make the entire world prosperous. Even if it makes the world prosperous, when it goes to the spirit world, it wants to help those who lived poorly in the past. Why is that? For God to be able to dwell, the timing must be right. Just as a servant must have a sense of timing to fulfill their role, there is a rhythm to this. 

So, do not even think about trying to see God. It was very good that God remained invisible. Instead, there is always a way for me to connect with God. That is enough, right? There is a way to whisper to Him. It’s just that you don’t know. Once you discover it, it cannot be given up. That taste is like the taste of honey. 

True People and the Construction of Heaven
Everyone, when bees taste honey, in winter they can only drink sugar water. However, when spring comes and they taste honey, no matter how much you pull their tails, they won’t let go. If insects are like this, how much more so when it comes to the love of God, where people are determined to live and die? Who would care if someone cuts off their neck? There is such a wonderful path. When it comes to love, it is not three but just two, right? That’s right. That is why God is in my heart, and He has an internal and external relationship with me. Our bodies are the house of God. 

When viewed this way, who are our human ancestors, Adam and Eve? They are God wearing a body. That’s how it is. God is in their hearts. This internal master and external master must be in complete harmony with each other, becoming the standard of peace in the universe and the absolute standard of happiness, from which the happiness of the world can be measured. 

If our human ancestors had not fallen, what would have happened? Our human ancestors are the body of God, and God, as the Lord who created the universe, is in our hearts. The God who wears a body and the internal God become one, living in a place where they love each other and their wills align. Then, when they die, they return to the world of the heart. 

What does dying mean? It means entering the world of the heart. It is to return to inherit an infinite stage of activity, not a world limited with God. The time when we shed this body is the time of death. If this body does not die, then the fear of death can be transcended without issue. 

One must become a person who stands in such a position to be a true person. However, there cannot be only men. There cannot be just one man. Has there been a woman in the escape until now? No, there hasn’t. That cannot be. In the future, there must also be women in the escape. Men and women must come together, not fighting over who is higher, but becoming one to fulfill the role of escape. That time is the ideal world, and it is the origin of the world where happiness can sing. Do you understand? 

In the Unification Church, we do not pray saying, "I pray in the name of Jesus." It is because it is one-sided, and we dislike that. So, we pray saying, "I pray in the name of True Parents." What is the fall? It is having false parents, isn’t it? Right? You were born with the bloodline of false parents who made mistakes. Therefore, for this to be made right, true parents must come and give birth again. That is why in the Unification Church, we pray in the name of True Parents. Do you understand? So, is it alone or together? "Together." 

If this is explained in detail, even Christians cannot do it. They will follow. People will follow if there is a more valuable path, a more beneficial path. There is no need for anyone to tell them to go. They will go on their own. The same goes for Unification Church members. They don’t know, but once they know, they will go without needing to be told. I have been doing this for over 50 years now. Does anyone tell me to go? I go because I cannot not go. 

You all know, but what is a true person? A person who becomes a son or daughter of God and establishes an internal and external relationship with God, standing in a place where the inside and outside are one. "You are you, and I am I." When the two become one, it is called the unity of husband and wife, right? The unity of internal and external is a decisive position where the expectations of the son-in-law can align. 

When true people, bound by human ethics and heavenly ethics, human affection and heavenly justice, create families on this earth, true families will emerge, and from those true families will come true tribes, true nations, and true worlds, right? It is absolutely impossible for only true individuals to emerge. Today, all those who believe in Jesus think they can go to heaven by believing alone, right? That is not the teaching of Jesus. That is why it comes down to earth. What is bound on earth will be bound in heaven. Because Jesus could not establish a true family, he is in paradise. He could not enter heaven. 

Originally, humans were meant to be in such a position, to form good families and live, and then the entire family would enter heaven. If the father goes to hell, the mother goes to heaven, the son goes to hell, and the daughter goes to heaven, what kind of heaven is that? Heaven is a place where not only families but also nations and entire peoples can align with the law. Because such nations have not emerged on this earth today, heaven has not yet become heaven. 

That is why our Unification Church aims to create heaven. Through families formed by true people aligned with God's love, we want to organize tribes, nations, and the world, creating a heaven centered on God. We must create heaven on this earth to go to the heaven of the other world. 

Only those who standardize and live this way will stand in a superior position that transcends all of history, establishing the authority of victory, and will not fall short of standing before God and all humanity. You must understand that this is the path you must take as true people. 

<Prayer> Beloved Father, as we seek to rise and rise and rise again, the ultimate destination is the place where we meet with You. 

When asked what the final decisive word is that You can say and we can say, it will be, "You are my son; I am your son." That is the word that humanity desires, and it is the decisive word for meeting the humanity You have come to find. 

It will not end with just meeting as sons and daughters; those sons and daughters are of Your bones and flesh, and their internal desires will manifest in us. The desires of an individual will manifest in a family, and the desires of a family will transcend society and nation, overflowing to all humanity, becoming the true internal feelings of Your true internal body, overflowing to a universally valid global standard. That world is the world of hope You are seeking, and it is the one world that humanity is striving for. 

From this perspective, we must look for whether there are groups in this historical age that are truly seeking this path. We must investigate. We must analyze and critique how much value we can find in our own selves to seek heavenly value and what equal position we should stand in with heaven. We must arrive at a decisive position where this must be done, standing before all people, all worlds, and the new trends, establishing a standard of truth that can guide them. 

The appearance of truth has been so in the past, is so in the present, and will be so in the future; no one can occupy or deny this. This transcends everything. 

Even fallen humans long for parental love, live according to the bonds of marriage, and wish to leave a future hope through their children. This family system of life becomes a medium that can connect the feelings of the fallen world and serves as the foundation of human ethics and affection. Similarly, for heavenly ethics and human ethics, heavenly justice and human affection to be bound together, we must establish a victorious family system on this earth that can connect the standards sought by saints with today’s human ethics. 

When we look at this fact, men and women must not become the same men and women as in the past. 

Fathers must be able to prove themselves, and we must have the conviction that we are the sons and daughters of the Father. Not only conviction but also from a compassionate position, we must prove that the Father and I are in a relationship of before and after, left and right, and from that position, we must discover ourselves capable of establishing the origin of the argument that we have been together eternally, live together eternally, and will live together eternally, without change. We have now come to know that this is the true path we must take. 

Father, now more than anyone, we must welcome You into our hearts. We must bring the Absolute Being, who cannot be invaded by anyone, into the place of our hearts, discuss with You, and discover the infinite value of our own existence in relation to the subjective Father. If there is a life that can live with this, no matter how evil the world may be, we will be able to create a new foundation of historical creation that can multiply infinite value within that evil realm. 

When we think of this, the suffering that person endures can be digested as happiness, and they are not unhappy people in a world filled with the waves of death but happy people living for happiness. 

The members of the Unification Church know that they must walk this path, so the path they have walked until now has been a path of suffering, a path of persecution, a lonely path. Yet, at every intersection where that persecution and loneliness intersected, the path we must take has been clear. 

To plant the bonds of value that humanity must have, not only through their own path but also through the paths that spread out and intersect in all directions, we reflect on the historical facts of the Unification Church, which struggled to leave the bonds of goodness. Although it was miserable, we thank You for placing us in a position where we can have a heart of gratitude that others do not know. 

In such a position, we must take root and cultivate a global foundation, dreaming of a new world that transcends Asia and the world, not only having a patriotic heart but also learning the way of loyalty according to the heavenly principles and the way of filial piety according to the heavenly principles, seeking a higher level of value. May Your blessing be with those who walk this path, and may they know that the increased value of their lives today is of a higher dimension than any value of those living in a flat world. May Your compassion and love be with them even more. 

No matter how evil the world may be, we know that the subjective power that must lead this evil world must be stronger and cannot be weak. We must not be lonely, and in times of loneliness, we must not be lonely in place of the Father’s strength and ability. We earnestly wish to be a group that influences this world. 

To Your beloved children who are attending in the Mapo district today, through this evening’s words, please evaluate their value highly, and allow them to become new beings with principled values established at the highest level that no one can pursue, whether they are men or women. 

This group, who feels more strongly than anyone that families, nations, and the world must become one centered around a world that cannot be divided, are the groups of unification in this era. 

When the Japanese, who were once enemies, come to have the name of family, they become brothers, and countless races of different colors can live with brotherly love centered around the name of family, which cannot be found among any nation. 

Such movements are taking root on this earth and are rushing toward practical stages. Father, please look upon this with compassion and increase the infinite strength and ability here, so that we may not become cowards but may embody the image of victors, boldly and courageously advancing as heavenly warriors. 

We entrust all of this to You, asking that You personally oversee the remaining time according to Your will, and we pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. *
